Editorial

Closing of the Meeting of Representatives of Chambers of Commerce from Various Provinces and Cities

The joint meeting of chambers of commerce from various provinces and cities has now concluded. The current meeting is nearly a decade from the last. In these years, the situation of industry and commerce has become more difficult and the encounters more severe. Externally, economic aggression presses hard. Internally, rural revival seems infinitely far off. Though this is an overall economic problem, which cannot be effectively resolved by local solutions, one should not succumb to others merely because the difficulties and dangers are great. Therefore, the holding of the current joint meeting of representatives of chambers of commerce from various provinces and cities is indeed a manifestation of the self-awareness of industry and commerce.

The meeting lasted three days. Though the period was short, the resolutions discussed, such as inspecting smuggled goods, the long-unresolved issue of the liability for repayment of partnership debts, and the abolition of disguised likin and postponement of income tax, all have a direct bearing on industry and commerce. Following these paths, though it may not be possible to revitalize industry and commerce in a positive sense, in a negative sense the protection can also maintain industry and commerce from collapsing. For rest and recuperation are indeed the way to revive the declining and revitalize the abandoned. Herewith, we will select the main points of the resolutions for discussion.

Though Shanghai is the first line of defense for the nation's commerce, it is difficult to fortify the front line if the rear is weak. Today's smuggling all targets the rear. The rear should have a strict organization so that the front may be free from worries about the rear. Since the chambers of commerce are representative organizations of industry and commerce in various places, the prevention of smuggling relies precisely on the automatic action of industry and commerce in various places. If they do not transport or sell them and strictly inspect and deal with them fairly, smuggled goods will be eliminated without being intercepted. Therefore, whether smuggling can be stopped in the future will depend on the strength of the anti-smuggling committees established this time in various places.

Everyone knows that industry and commerce have been exhausted in recent years. The abolition of harsh levies and the elimination of likin are measures to revive them. However, due to the financial difficulties of local governments, the so-called "disguised likin" is still difficult to completely abolish, and the promulgation of new taxes imposes an even heavier burden. Taxes come from the people. The reason for the current financial difficulties is precisely because the people are poor and merchants are distressed. Inland commerce is far inferior to the past due to the bankruptcy of the countryside, frequent droughts and floods, and the result of banditry. The people have no purchasing power, goods are accumulated and immobile, and funds are concentrated in the cities. The turnover is difficult, and the market is even more desolate. The business tax, special tax, and house tax are all burdensome compared to their current ability. Moreover, now that income tax is levied in addition to business tax, though income is taken from profits and is not comparable to those who must bear it regardless of profit or loss, even if there is a surplus in one year, it all comes from saving on expenses. A slight expansion is bound to be unsustainable. In addition, the accounting organization of inland stores is crude and simple, and there is no telling what disputes will arise in the future from uncovering concealment and auditing net profits.

The issue of liability for partnership operations has been debated for a long time. From a legal point of view, it is fair that each partner should be jointly responsible for the amount by which the partnership assets are insufficient to pay off the partnership debts. In fact, the liability of shareholders in limited liability companies is limited to their invested capital. Before the company business is developed, partnership operations still account for the majority of business organizations. It is impossible to force them all to reorganize uniformly. The original intention of the legislation was to protect the interests of creditors, but the opposite often happens. Because of the need for joint responsibility, the more wealthy partners are unwilling to contribute their due share of capital, waiting for the situation to change. As a result, lawsuits drag on for years, and people run around mediating. The creditors' gains may not be enough to compensate for their losses. If the amount of the shortfall is allowed to be apportioned according to shares to complete their responsibility, those who care about their reputation will all be happy to pay. For those who do not pay, strict sanctions should be set, and creditors should also be able to seek legal remedies for relief. Moreover, because of the great responsibility borne by partners, the more wealthy partners regard engaging in industry and commerce as a dangerous prospect, and deposit all their funds abroad. Inland finance is becoming more and more depleted. If the responsibility for partnership repayment can be slightly reduced, then the investment in industry and commerce will not be as hesitant as before.

However, all this is not a problem for the chambers of commerce themselves. I believe that what the chambers of commerce in various places should pay the most attention to today is how to develop their spirit. Is the purpose of the chambers of commerce not to seek the development of industry, commerce, and foreign trade? At a time when trade is in deficit and there is no way out, export commodities remain the same as before, foreign forces are encroaching deeper and deeper, handicrafts have failed and are on the verge of exhaustion, and new industries have no way to take their place, the laxity of the industrial and commercial sectors is still as old as ever, and the dispersion of the spirit is still like that of the elderly. But ordinary merchants still regard the group as a tool to deal with government offices. As for the improvement of business and the creation of enterprises, they often close their doors and refuse to join the forces of the group and are unwilling to have it interfere. Therefore, not only has foreign trade not benefited from development, but how can there be any development of the industrial and commercial sectors themselves? Therefore, whether the healthy development of industry and commerce is possible in the future, the key lies in whether the organization of industrial and commercial groups can be sound.

Half-Yuan Silver Coins Still Worth Five Jiao

(Nanjing) The three central banks jointly wrote to the Ministry of Finance, stating that the Yuan Shikai half-yuan coins cast by the Jiangzhe Mint have always been used as five jiao for foreign silver dollars. When the three banks collect them, they should still be calculated as two coins exchanged for one yuan. The Ministry of Finance replied in approval. (22nd Central News Agency Dispatch)

Lei Zhen Returns to Beijing from Jiangxi Yesterday

Chinese Detective of Japanese Consulate Police Station in Tianjin Shot Dead; Incident Occurs in Front of the Tianjin Municipal Government; Cause Due to Misunderstanding; Japanese Consulate Authorities Protest

(Tianjin) A certain important incident occurred at the Jingang Bridge in front of the Tianjin Municipal Government at 1:00 PM on the 22nd. The municipal authorities are currently negotiating with the Japanese side to resolve it peacefully. It is not expected to escalate. (22nd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Japanese consular authorities here have protested the shooting death of a police detective from the consulate by the municipal government guards. The remains of the detective have been removed by the Japanese police station. Representatives from the Japanese consulate, military authorities, and the military police have all been dispatched to the scene of the incident to investigate. (22nd Reuters Dispatch)

(Tianjin) A Chinese detective from the Japanese Consulate Police Station in Tianjin was shot dead by the guards of the Tianjin Municipal Government this afternoon. It is said that the detective had arrested a member of the municipal government guards in the Japanese concession. Later, he took him to the Hebei area in the city for investigation, and the trouble started from there. When the car carrying the detective and the arrested guard approached the gate of the municipal government, the guard on duty fired at the car, and the detective died on the spot. It is said that this accident was due to a misunderstanding. The guards on duty heard someone shouting loudly in the car and saw a struggle in the car, mistakenly thinking that their colleague was being kidnapped, so they opened fire, resulting in this disaster. (22nd Reuters Dispatch)

Song Zheyuan Inspects Feng Zhi'an's Troops

Liang Shitang Arrives in Beiping Yesterday

He returned to Beiping this morning after completing the matter. Liang said that he went to Beijing this time to report to Chiang Kai-shek. He stayed in Beijing for more than ten days. Chiang has now gone to Lushan for summer vacation, so he returned north to handle trivial matters. He is scheduled to visit Song Zheyuan tomorrow for a talk. (22nd Dispatch)

No News of Kawagoe's Trip North for the Time Being

Arino is also scheduled to go to Jinan in the middle of next month to take office as consul-general. (22nd Dispatch)

Japanese Troops Conduct Tactical Exercises at Lugou Bridge; Kawabe Inspects Troops Stationed in Fengtai

(Beiping) Lieutenant General Kawabe, the Japanese resident in Beiping, went to Fengtai this morning to inspect the stationed troops and then went to inspect the vicinity. At the same time, more than 100 officers and soldiers stationed there opened up to the Lugou Bridge and Changxindian area this morning with machine guns and field artillery to conduct tactical exercises. They returned to Fengtai for defense after completing the exercises in the afternoon. During the exercises, the traffic within a few miles of the area was temporarily blocked. The residents in the southwest of Beiping City could faintly hear the rumbling of artillery and intermittent gunfire. (22nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) More than 100 Japanese soldiers stationed in Beiping, led by the Japanese military attache, went to Jingshan Park for a tour this morning and returned to the camp at noon. (22nd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Kawabe, the commander of the Japanese brigade stationed in Beiping, went to Tianjin with Mutaguchi, the commander of the military police, at 9:25 AM on the 22nd to visit Tashiro and ask for instructions. (22nd Central News Agency Dispatch)

Japan Decides to Invest in Developing the Economy of North China

(Tianjin) Ishii, a senior staff officer of the Japanese Garrison in North China, stated that the safety of North China is related to Japan's national defense. Japan does not want this area to become a "desert" and be greatly affected. Therefore, it has decided to invest in developing the economy to stabilize the lives of North China's farmers, revitalize the rural areas, and promote market prosperity so that Japanese goods can be sold. This is a necessary measure for Japan; otherwise, Japan fears that the rural areas of North China will decline daily, and security and economy will be shaken, affecting Japan's national defense policy. He dared to declare that Japan has absolutely no intention of making North China a "Manchukuo" the second. The treasures and underground resources within Shanxi Province, coupled with the poverty of the people and the exhaustion of wealth, would also benefit the province if Japan were to invest. The construction of the Cangshi Railway and the economy of Hebei Province are also of great importance. The military is pursuing this plan and is seriously monitoring Japanese investors who engage in deceptive practices. (22nd Dispatch)

Shiozawa Holds Police Conference in Tianjin

(Tianjin) Police officers from the Beining Railway and the Japanese police stations in Peiping and Tianjin held a meeting at the Japanese Consulate General Police Station in Tianjin at 10:00 AM on the 22nd. The meeting centered around Shiozawa, a police inspector from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Over thirty people, including the police chief of Tianjin, Wakuitsutsu, and the deputy Japanese Consul, Nishida, participated. Matters regarding expanding police authority, establishing police substations along the Peiping-Hankou and Tianjin-Pukou Railways, and the cohabitation of Japanese and Korean people were discussed and decisions were made. The meeting continued at 2:00 PM and concluded in the evening. Police officers from each substation left Tianjin on the morning of the 23rd. (23rd Dispatch)

Smuggled Hankou Goods to Disappear; Instructions Sought on How to Handle Confiscated Goods; Legitimate Duty-Paid Japanese Goods Are Steadily Being Transported to Hankou

(Hankou) Since the establishment of the Anti-Smuggling Headquarters, the smuggling routes southward have been cut off. The crackdown along the Peiping-Hankou Railway is particularly stringent. Starting from June 2nd, branch offices were established in Dazhimen, Xinyang, Zhumadian, Xuchang, Zhengzhou, Xinxiang, Shijiazhuang, and Changxindian to intercept the southward smuggling route. Those without transportation and sales licenses were detained. As a result, a surprisingly large amount of confiscated smuggled sugar, bicycle parts, aniline dyes, and rayon has been seized. The Customs is currently seeking instructions from the headquarters on how to handle these items. The Anti-Smuggling Headquarters has also sent Deputy Director Li Shoupeng to Hankou to oversee everything. Currently, most Chinese merchants in Wuhan have realized that trafficking in smuggled goods is nothing but self-inflicted suffering. Due to the significant losses from mid-way confiscations, most have voluntarily stopped. With the reduction in the source of smuggled goods, the need for legitimate duty-paid Japanese goods in the market has become urgent. Recently, these goods have been transported to Hankou by Japanese ships. For example, Japanese ships on the Yangtze River had not imported sugar for three months, but recently, it has been arriving steadily. The "Luoyang Maru," which arrived in Hankou the other day, transported 4,000 bags of white sugar. From this, it can be seen that the Chinese authorities' anti-smuggling efforts are directly promoting the development of normal trade between China and Japan. (22nd Central News Agency Dispatch)

Page 7

The Overall Situation in Spain Remains Chaotic; The Rebel Army Tenaciously Resists; The Government's 150,000-Strong Army Advances Northward; The Time for a Major Battle Is Imminent

(Paris) The situation in Spain remains unclear. Both the government and the rebel army claim victory. It is not easy for outsiders to know the truth. According to news from Madrid, the situation there is relatively peaceful. However, almost all the troops in the city have been transferred to the northern and southern fronts to confront the rebel army. According to news from Andaye (southern France), the border between France and Spain was quiet last night. According to the observations of French authorities in that city, the rebel army is likely to start negotiations with the government army first to persuade them to surrender. If negotiations fail, they will launch an attack. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) The latest news from Spain received here states that the Spanish government has dispatched 150,000 troops to advance northward to prevent the rebel army from moving south. This army includes troops loyal to the government, militias, and youth leagues of socialists and communists. It is expected that this will be a decisive battle between the government and the rebel army. The report also stated that the rebel army will engage in battle in the area of the Somosierra Pass, which is the main mountain pass of the rebel army.

(Paris) Police along the French-Spanish border reported today that the rebel army led by General Mola had taken San Sebastian without a fight, occupying many villages along the way. It is claimed that Mr. Mola announced that as soon as he was certain that the north supported the rebel army, he would launch an attack on Madrid. Now, the time for a major battle seems imminent because members of the Popular Front in that area have begun to arm themselves to assist the government. (21st Nationalist Electric)

Madrid The government issued a broadcast message at 7:00 AM today, stating that rebel forces across the country have been defeated. The fighting between government and rebel forces only persists in the outskirts of Zaragoza, Seville, and Valladolid. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

Madrid Interior Minister General Pozas issued a broadcast message stating that the leader of the rebel army in Zaragoza, Cabanellas (the former commander of the Fifth Division), had issued a general mobilization order in the area. All conscripts from the 1931 and 1936 classes must enlist today. The government views this move as a sign that the rebel army is running out of steam. (22nd Havas Dispatch) (Paris) According to various sources, the Spanish rebel army is gradually making significant progress. Refugees arriving at Hendaye on the French-Spanish border claim that the provinces of Zaragoza, Navarre, Caca, Vitoria, Burgos, Valladolid, and Pontevedra are all under rebel control. Border guards in Hendaye, Biarritz, and Danquieria have also sided with the rebel army. The rebel army has now occupied San Sebastian, but the radio station has not yet surrendered and is currently under siege by the rebel army. At the same time, according to news from Tangier, the rebel headquarters in Ceuta has warned neutral ships to leave the port because the rebel army plans to bomb government warships from the air. It is said that the ships are trapped in the port due to lack of fuel and food. However, one British warship remains in the port. (22nd Reuters Dispatch)

The Authorities of Catalonia Issue a Warning to the Rebel Army, Urging Them to Withdraw from the City of Zaragoza, Otherwise They Will Dispatch the Air Force to Bomb

Barcelona According to general knowledge, the authorities are scheduled to organize a military court today or tomorrow at the latest to try the arrested rebel leaders, many of whom will be sentenced to death. Lieutenant Colonel Sandino, the commander of the Air Force in this city, issued a warning to General Cabanellas, the leader of the rebel army in Zaragoza, by radio this morning, stating that if the regime in that city is not handed over to a civilian governor loyal to the government within a short period of time, a detachment of the Air Force will fly to the city to bomb the barracks. The situation in this city is still stable, and food supplies can still be maintained as usual. According to newspaper reports, all organizations that do not support the republican system have been ordered to be closed by the provincial government. The authorities have taken over all churches and monuments of artistic value and posted a notice in front of the doors stating, "This place has been taken over by the government to open public welfare institutions." For example, all the churches owned by the Franciscan Church have been converted into hospitals. General Goded, one of the rebel leaders, and most of the rebellious officers are currently detained in this church after being arrested. Colonel Sangfeliz, the former adjutant of General Barerra, the rebel staff officer, is also among them. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

Warships Concentrated in the Port of Tangier Awaiting Orders, the Navy and Air Force Fiercely Bomb Ceuta, One Rebel Ship Sunk by a Submarine

Tangier Twelve Spanish warships are currently docked in this port. It is said that as soon as the "Jaime I" battleship arrives, it will bombard the rebel army in Ceuta. Rebel leader Franco requested today that the International Committee governing Tangier order the warships to withdraw or submit to the rebel army, otherwise rebel aircraft will bomb the warships. However, the position of the "Jaime I" is quite questionable. The ship has a displacement of 16,000 tons, a crew of 854, and is armed with eight 12-inch guns. Rebel leader General Mola announced by radio that the ship had arrived in Vigo and joined the rebel army. News from Vigo, on the other hand, stated that the ship's commander did intend to join the rebellion, but the soldiers refused and shot the commander. (21st Nationalist Electric)

French Oran, North Africa The entire Spanish territory of Morocco is currently under the control of the rebel army. Yesterday morning, four government warships loyal to the government opened fire and bombarded Ceuta. The rebel army in the area immediately returned fire, and both sides fired many shots. The warships then retreated. At 2:00 PM, a government aircraft flew to the city and dropped bombs. Currently, the French government has increased its troop strength along the border of its North African territory to prevent incidents. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

(London) Reuters reports that a correspondent in Tangier stated that a submarine loyal to the Spanish government sank the rebel gunboat "Dato" today. (21st Nationalist Electric)

Tense Situation in the North; San Sebastian Falls into the Hands of the Rebel Army

(London) According to news received from the French border, the town of San Sebastian in northern Spain has been occupied by the rebel army after fierce fighting. Twenty-four members of the local loyalist short-gun team were killed in the battle. Several British travelers drove several cars from there across the French border. It is believed that several British people are still stranded in the area. After the rebel army succeeded, it is said that it is now advancing southwest towards Bilbao, the capital of the province of Biscay. According to British travelers arriving at Hendaye on the French-Spanish border, San Sebastian was attacked by rebel aircraft from the sky with machine guns before it surrendered. At the same time, the rebel army's attempt to invade Madrid has failed. The government army fought the rebel army twice near the capital and defeated the rebel army. Those who participated in the battle included the assault police force, city guards, and Red Militia. (22nd Reuters Dispatch)

(Paris) Well-informed sources have recently stated that the provinces of Navarre and Guipuzcoa in northern Spain, and most of the province of Andalusia in the south, are all in the hands of the rebel army. The rebel army is currently advancing on the capital, Madrid, in two directions, north and south. The northern army is led by General Mola, which includes the regular army originally stationed in the northern provinces, the militias of the cities of Burgos and Zaragoza, and members of the Traditionalist Communion party (also known as the "Carlist Party") of Pamplona (whose leader is Prince Carlos, who is 86 years old and opposes the restoration of King Alfonso XIII). The general's long-cherished wish is to move south, and claims to be only 50 kilometers away from the capital, Madrid. General Mola also told reporters that his actions are purely for the sake of national interest, and his goal is to liberate Spain from the scourge of Marxist factions, the Second and Third Internationals, and various secret societies. The southern army is led by General Franco, the commander-in-chief of the rebel army, whose troops are mostly the Seville city garrison, but it is reported that they have been surrounded by the government army of Malaga and Rijonté and the Mediterranean coast, so their position is quite dangerous.

The above is the situation of the rebel army in mainland Spain. As for the government side, it recently announced that the rebel army in Alcalá de Henares and Tetuán in the vicinity of the capital had been defeated by the government troops, suffering heavy casualties. Moroccan rebels landing at Algeciras (not far from the British port of Gibraltar) were also repelled by the government army.

However, generally speaking, the current situation in northern Spain is indeed extremely tense. A large number of officials in that area have crossed the border to France to take refuge, and have visited French officials. Among them are the governors of the three provinces of Navarre, Guipuzcoa, and Pamplona, and the leaders of the Popular Front in Irún, Irazki, etc., as well as more than 50 British expatriates, carrying their wives, children, and luggage, and traveling on trucks placed by the Popular Front to take refuge in France. It is now known that the rebel army led by General Mola encountered the government army in Entarraje near the French border and engaged in a fierce battle. The government army suffered 24 deaths and retreated in defeat. A bridge in Entarraje was destroyed to prevent the rebel army from advancing. The rebel army took a secluded path and went straight to the city of San Sebastian, and finally captured it at 5:10 PM and immediately took advantage of the victory to advance west and seize the port of Bilbao (on the coast of the Bay of Biscay). At the same time, Irún has also been surrounded by the rebel army, but according to news received in Bayonne (southern France), the San Sebastian radio station is still in the hands of the government army. It is also said that the northern industrial center of Bilbao was occupied by the rebel army at 10:30 PM tonight. In addition, a Colonel Villanubia led 400 "Carlists" from Pamplona along the Bidasoa River to Behobia. The garrison of Behobia, mostly communists, destroyed the bridge to prevent the rebel army from advancing. The rebel army has crossed the river and advanced to 10 kilometers from the city, waiting for reinforcements from the rear before attacking the troops inside the city. Trenches have been dug in the mountains near Irún and Behobia, winding and undulating, stretching endlessly, for defense. According to news received in Andaye (also in southern France), the provinces of Navarre, Guipuzcoa, Burgos, and Valladolid in northern Spain are now in the hands of the rebel army. Two policemen from the province of Pamplona recently escaped to Andaye across the border. According to them, when the rebel army entered San Sebastian, they witnessed the gendarmes in the city immediately surrendering and not resisting. A section of the border between France and Spain is now guarded by the rebel army. It is also rumored that a portion of the Barcelona city garrison in Spain mutinied. The local government has asked the capital for assistance. (21st Havas Dispatch)

Violent Street Fighting Erupts in Barcelona; 300 Dead, 3,000 Injured; Authorities Announce Martial Law

(Paris) The correspondent of the evening newspaper in Barcelona stated that the fierce fighting in the Rambla area on Monday resulted in 300 deaths and 3,000 injuries. Several chapels and monasteries were burned down at the time. (21st Nationalist Electric)

Barcelona According to a statement issued by the authorities last night, the workers of this city, with the assistance of the security forces, fought fiercely with the rebels. From last Saturday to yesterday, the rebels were finally defeated. Order in this city has now returned to peace. It is reported that Valencia is also peaceful and uneventful. The local radio station issued a warning to the rebel commander in Zaragoza at 2:30 this morning, stating that if they do not immediately surrender to the government army, they will be bombed. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

(London) According to a report from a Daily Telegraph correspondent, the Spanish rebel army has occupied Barcelona again. (21st Nationalist Electric)

(Paris) According to the latest news received here, the Spanish rebel army occupied Barcelona this morning. It is said that civilians and policemen attached to the rebel army fought street battles with armed soldiers all day long. In the early morning, when the rebel army entered the city, they disbanded all the policemen and armed soldiers, but they could not find the Communist Party Executive Committee. The state news reported that the fall of Barcelona was welcomed by the people because the three days of terror had come to an end. The rebel army has a significant advantage in northern Spain, and it is reported that ten provinces are in their hands. (22nd Nationalist Electric)

The Rebel Party's Uprising Plan; Simultaneous Attacks on the Borders Were Discovered in Advance; The Failure of the Militia to Rebel Was a Major Reason for the Divine Defeat

Madrid The outbreak of this rebellion in Spain has become a prairie fire in just a few days. It is known that the rebel party's conspiracy to launch an uprising must not have been a matter of a day or two. However, until now, the content of their plan has begun to be revealed. It is reported that the rebel party's original plan was to launch simultaneous attacks in various border areas (Seville in the south, San Sebastian in the north, and Barcelona in the east), converging on the capital to make the government caught off guard, and the regime would be readily available. However, since the air force did not rebel, and most of the security forces remained loyal to the government, a part of the above plan was foiled. In addition, many rebel generals and officers used the excuse that the republican system was threatened since the Popular Front cabinet came to power, and persuaded the soldiers to rebel. The soldiers were unaware for a while and were given what they were. Now, most have realized that they have defected after the militia of the Popular Front won, and this is another reason why the rebel party's plan has been hit. Currently, the government army and the rebel party are still at war, and the situation is more intense than ever. Although the government wants to quickly put out the flames of the rebellion, this rebellion will have a profound impact on the political situation in Spain, and there are fears that it is something that the authorities cannot foresee. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

The Truth About the Rebellion in the South; The Port of Almería Is Said to Be Recaptured

Madrid Telephone communication between here and Barcelona has been restored, and the truth about the rebellion in the south has been learned in detail for the first time. A retrospective account is as follows: This mutiny was led by General Goded. The participants included 5,000 soldiers and some civilians. General Galasco, the commander of the Catalonia garrison, issued martial law after the alarm was raised in Morocco. The rebel army originally planned to attack on Saturday morning, but their conspiracy was detected by the police, and the police deployed machine guns in advance at key locations to stand by. Fierce street fighting broke out between the University Square, Catalonia Square, and between Carrer de les Corts Catalanes and Diputació, and bloody battles also broke out in front of the barracks. From 10:00 to 11:00 on Sunday morning, the garrison and the police repeatedly engaged in hand-to-hand combat with the rebel army in order to prevent the rebel army from invading other places. Colonel Sandino also led five aircraft to assist the government army in quelling the rebellion. The Communist Party also joined the government army in combat. (21st Nationalist Electric)

Rabat, French Morocco, North Africa The port of Almería in southern Spain has been recaptured by the government army. The details of the process are worth mentioning. First, the Spanish cruiser "Libertad" arrived at the British port of Gibraltar from the port of Tangier in North Africa and planned to refuel there, but was refused by the British authorities. The ship then sailed to the port of Almería (then in the hands of the rebel army) and was able to assist the government army in opening fire and bombarding the rebel army. After a fierce battle between the two sides, the port was finally recaptured. General Deliano, the leader of the rebel army in Seville and commander of the Andalusia Division, upon hearing the news, has dispatched reinforcements to the port in an attempt to counterattack. The rest of Seville province remained calm this morning. The local military authorities have taken various measures to ensure that food supplies are not cut off. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

The Capital Restores to Normal; Most of the Militias Were Transferred Away

Madrid The capital was still peaceful last night. Most of the fires were extinguished this morning. Most of the militias have been transferred to the three cities of Valladolid, Burgos, and Zaragoza to suppress the rebel army, and the militias left to guard the capital have been greatly reduced. According to news from Huelva, three clergy there attacked Marxist party members and declared their support for the Fascist Party and were arrested by the civilian administrator. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

Madrid The situation in the capital was restored to normal last night. Many rioters who opened fire on passers-by were arrested by the military police. Seventy percent of the militias in the capital have boarded trucks and gone to the northern and southern fronts to suppress the rebel army. Interior Minister Pozas declared at 1:00 this morning that the cities of Gijón, Almería, and Alcalá de Henares (all near the capital) had been recaptured by the government army, and several rebel leaders were arrested in Alcalá de Henares. Currently, only the three cities of Zaragoza, Valladolid, and Seville are still in the hands of the rebel army. A column of government troops has set out from Barcelona, ​​preparing to recapture Zaragoza, while Seville has also been surrounded by the government army. By 4:00 this morning, official sources declared that the rebel army in Seville had been completely defeated and had surrendered to the government. In addition, the government army defeated a rebel army in the Guadarrama Mountains, 100 kilometers north of the capital. The rebel army immediately hid in the Somosierra tunnel for cover. The government of Toledo reported to the government that the rebels there were fleeing to Alcalá de Henares (southeast of Madrid) in dire straits and would be captured in their entirety soon. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

Britain and the United States Send Warships to Protect Overseas Chinese; Sailors from Britain, France, and Italy Ordered to Land in Tangier

(London) In view of the tense situation in Spain, the British and American governments are now sending warships to various ports in the country to protect their overseas Chinese. According to a Washington dispatch, two American warships were ordered to go to the Mediterranean today. The American battleship "Oklahoma," which is currently docked in Cherbourg, France, has been ordered to contact the American ambassador to Madrid, Bowers, and, if necessary, will carry American expatriates out of the country. The British authorities have sent a cruiser to Barcelona, and another to Palma on Mallorca. The cruiser "Amphion," which left the UK yesterday to join the African Fleet, has been ordered to go to the port of Tenerife in the Canary Islands. The battlecruiser "Repulse," which is carrying the Gordon Highlanders garrisoned in Alexandria back to Gibraltar, is preparing to load British overseas Chinese in Spanish ports if necessary. (22nd Reuters Dispatch)

(London) The British cruiser "Taurus" has sailed to Palma in Spain, and the cruiser "London" is approaching Barcelona. The submarine flotilla flagship "Douglas" and three destroyers will join her tomorrow. The destroyer "Boadicea" has been ordered to go to Alicante, and the destroyer "Basilisk" is now heading towards Almería. (22nd Reuters Dispatch)

Tangier Sailors from British, French, and Italian warships have now been ordered to land to replace the local police and protect the consulates of their respective countries. Because the rebel party had threatened to bomb the entire city, the local people were extremely panicked. There are currently nine government warships docked in the port, and three government cruisers anchored near Gibraltar. It is believed that the ships plan to bombard Algeciras tonight. (22nd Reuters Dispatch)

Sailing from Gibraltar to Tangier, Bombs Dropped by Airplane Landed Only a Few Yards from Stern

Gibraltar - The British company steamer "One Achille Lauro" set sail from here today for Tangier when it encountered danger, narrowly escaping disaster. A Spanish airplane dropped several bombs, which landed only forty yards from the ship's stern. (Reuters, 22nd)

Spanish Civil War Closely Watched by London, Deep Concern About Impact on Portuguese Political Situation

(London) Political figures here are closely watching the developments in Spain, deeply concerned that Portugal may be affected. It is feared that if the parties of the Spanish Popular Front are able to quell the rebellion, the leftist parties in Portugal will be encouraged to revolt against the government led by the current President Carmona and Prime Minister Salazar. Historically, Britain and Portugal cooperate in emergencies and maintain friendly relations. The Portuguese government also grants British warships preferential rights in Portuguese territorial waters. If the current Portuguese government is overthrown, the existing relationship between Britain and Portugal will be severely harmed. (Havas, 21st)

Outer Mongolia's Military Preparedness Sufficient to Resist Foreign Invasion, Celebration of Republic's Founding in Kulun

(London) According to a Daily Telegraph correspondent in Moscow, Kulun is currently holding celebrations simultaneously commemorating the alliance between Russia and Mongolia and the 15th anniversary of the founding of the Republic of Outer Mongolia. Soviet representative Ilyaeva stated today, "The friendship and mutual assistance between the Soviet Union and Outer Mongolia, united by the passionate blood of the fine sons and daughters of the Mongolian nation," has existed since the founding of Mongolia and did not begin with the public announcement of the alliance between the two countries on March 12th. The Mongolian army and air force are now undergoing training in a new era. Airplane pilots, tank crews, and artillery officers are all Mongolians, and new industries have been established, with 80% of the workers, hundreds of instructors, and foremen being Mongolian. Mongolian Prime Minister Amor declared that the Mongolian army has recently been greatly increased, military equipment has also been improved, and the salaries of officers and political personnel in the army have been doubled. (Reuters, 22nd)

Japanese Air Defense Drill, Tokyo Imposes Blackout

(Tokyo) The air defense exercises in the three major cities of Tokyo, Osaka, and Yokohama have reached their final stage today. The simulated large enemy aircraft squadrons are approaching Tokyo. A night air raid will be carried out tonight, so 230,000 members of the Tokyo defense corps have been actively mobilized since this morning. Princes Asaka and Higashikuni also personally inspected the preparations. The atmosphere in Tokyo tonight is very tense, and it will become a world of darkness. (United Press, 22nd)

Representatives from Britain, France, and Belgium Begin Talks in London This Morning, Discussing Solutions to the General European Situation, Preparing for Future Five-Power Conference, Britain Advocates Realism and is Willing to Accommodate Germany

(London) The talks between Britain, France, and Belgium are scheduled to begin at 10:30 AM tomorrow at the Prime Minister's residence at 10 Downing Street. The British representatives are Prime Minister Baldwin, Foreign Secretary Eden, and Lord Privy Seal Halifax. The French representatives are Prime Minister Blum and Foreign Minister Delbos. The Belgian representatives are Prime Minister Janson and Foreign Minister Spaak. Foreign Secretary Eden will also host a luncheon for the French and Belgian representatives tomorrow. (Havas, 22nd)

(London) Regarding the holding of a second Locarno Conference, Britain, France, and Belgium have each issued communiqués in their respective capitals. It is learned that while the British government has accepted the wording of the communiqués this morning, it still insists that the talks being held in London are only preliminary in nature, and that the term "conference" should be reserved for the five-power meeting of Britain, France, Belgium, Germany, and Italy to be held in Brussels next month. At this time, it would be more accurate to refer to the gathering of the three countries' representatives as "talks." The current cabinet places the greatest emphasis on the future five-power conference, not the three-power talks. It also believes that efforts are continuing to find ways to involve Germany in jointly resolving the general European situation. Therefore, while the mutual assistance obligations previously offered by France and Belgium, namely the military assistance measures stipulated in the annex to the first Locarno Conference agreement in March of this year, remain effective, they should not be regarded as permanent. After the five-power conference is held, it is necessary to first ascertain Germany's true intentions regarding various European issues before proceeding to seek a solution to the general European situation. The main goal of current British foreign policy is to restore the Locarno Treaty system and include Germany and Italy in it, so that Europe does not split into two groups and create a confrontational situation. (Havas, 20th)

(London) Members of Parliament in the parliament lounge recently stated that the most important issue discussed by the representatives of Britain, France, and Belgium is the issue of German troops stationed in the Rhineland. The French government is determined not to accept this fait accompli. The British government, on the other hand, is committed to realism and believes that continuing to insist on German troop withdrawal is futile and should be abandoned. (Havas, 21st)

Demilitarized Straits, Turkey Builds Fortresses, Fortifies Two Islands in Aegean Sea

Dardanelles - The Turkish ship "Yavuz," originally the famous German cruiser "Goeben" from World War I, today led a small Turkish fleet deep into the Dardanelles Strait, preparing to reoccupy the islands of Rhodes and Tenedos in the Aegean Sea. As a result of the Montreux Convention, which allows Turkey to immediately rearm the Dardanelles Strait, defensive works will be rebuilt on these two islands. (Reuters, 21st)

Danzig to Take Further Steps, Demanding Autonomous Rights, Guaranteeing Polish Interests in Exchange

Austria to Grant General Amnesty to Political Prisoners, 4,000-5,000 People to Benefit, First Step in Implementing German-Austrian Agreement

(Vienna) It is expected that Chancellor Schuschnigg will announce a general amnesty on July 24th, benefiting a total of 4,000-5,000 members of the Nazi Party, Socialist Party, and Communist Party. Additionally, the trials of 10,000 people accused of political crimes have been suspended. (Reuters, 22nd)

(Vienna) Following the recent conclusion of the German-Austrian Agreement, it is now being implemented. The first step is for the Austrian government to pardon all political prisoners, whether they are members of the Nazi Party or the Socialist Party, or the Communist Party. The total number is expected to be several thousand. Those included in the amnesty include former envoy to Italy, Linden (who was nominated by Nazi Party members as a candidate for Chancellor when Chancellor Dollfuss was assassinated on July 25, 1934), former Vienna police chief Starhemberg (both Nazi Party members), and former Vienna Mayor Seitz, a leader of the Social Democratic Party. In addition, the German government had previously issued an order requiring tourists visiting Austria to pay a tax of 1,000 marks to restrict Germans from traveling to Austria. This measure will be abolished by the German government. Other steps will be decided and implemented by the authorities of the two countries within this month. (Havas, 21st)

Czech-German-Austrian Relations, Messengers Going Back and Forth, Britain and France Anxious

French Infant Bonds, Enthusiastic Subscription Nationwide, Economy Trending Towards Prosperity

(Paris) French Finance Minister Valliot, in an exclusive interview with a Reuters reporter today, stated that the recent issuance of "infant bonds" by the government has been extremely satisfactory. Even citizens from impoverished classes are buying them. The national economic situation has now recovered, and a day of prosperity is coming soon. Sales in major Parisian stores have increased in the past two weeks, and this activity has greatly helped bond sales. Valliot also stated that the Bank of France has reduced the discount rate from 6% to 3% since June 15th. At the same time, the price of public bonds has gradually increased, and the outflow of gold has returned to the national treasury. Regarding the new measures for declaring overseas deposits, Valliot issued a warning, stating that after the amnesty expires on August 23rd, the law will not be lenient towards those who violate this law again. Valliot concluded, "Hope is now gradually being realized. If economic activity can increase its pace as we hope, France's finances will definitely recover." (Reuters, 21st)

Abyssinians Not Giving Up, Attempting to Recover Capital, Abyssinian General Leads Troops to Spy on Abyssinian Capital, Italian Troops Engage, Heavy Casualties

US Large-Scale Silver Purchases

Still Unable to Achieve Goals of Silver Purchase Act, Gold-Silver Ratio Increasingly Distant

(Washington) The Department of Commerce released a report today stating that although the US government has made large-scale silver purchases, it has still been unable to achieve the goals of the Silver Purchase Act, reducing the gold-silver ratio. Cash imports this year have reached $519,612,415 so far, more than four times the amount of silver imports during the same period. Therefore, the United States has failed in its goal to achieve a gold-silver ratio of 3:1. Silver imports this year have reached $120,493,167 so far. Although domestically produced silver is not included in this figure, the Bureau of Mines estimates that the government has purchased only $35,000,000 worth of domestically produced silver, while it has purchased $129,000,000 worth of domestically produced gold during the same period. Therefore, the gold-silver ratio has become increasingly distant. (National Telegraph, 21st)

Japanese Army Authorities to Reform Current Gendarmerie System

(Tokyo) In view of the recent serious situation, the Army authorities have decided to reform the military police system. The current Japanese gendarmerie system was implemented by order in the 31st year of Meiji and is under the jurisdiction of the Minister of the Army, performing both military police and administrative judicial police functions. However, the current gendarmerie organization is unable to fully implement these tasks, so it is being greatly reformed to prevent illegal incidents within the Army. The recent frequent occurrence of espionage incidents and other military administrative and judicial police incidents will be improved by increasing the number of gendarmerie, selecting outstanding individuals from active-duty officers, and sending them to the Imperial University or other universities to receive education, so as to cultivate gendarmerie that can adapt to the times. (Allied Press, 22nd)

Tianjin Customs Strictly Enforces Anti-Smuggling Measures, Strictly Prevents Smugglers from Hijacking Goods

(Tianjin) At 12:00 midnight on the 11th, more than fifty members of the smuggling ronin trade association heard that customs officers at the Xin Zhan had seized private goods being transported south. They immediately rushed to the station in a heavy-duty vehicle. Military police stationed at the station prevented them from entering the platform. The ronin lingered outside the station for a long time and were unable to enter. Until 2:00 AM on the 22nd, the last car of the seized private goods was being transported from Xin Zhan to the customs warehouse. Chief Customs Commissioner Hélia personally went to the station to supervise the loading and transport. To prevent the ronin from hijacking the goods, the goods were transported through Xiaoguan in the French Concession via Hebei. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) The customs anti-smuggling team today confiscated a large batch of smuggled goods transported by train from Tianjin to various inland areas. This is the first large-scale smuggling incident since smuggling began in North China. Last night, a large number of Koreans at Tianjin East Station loaded smuggled goods such as rayon, white sugar, and piece goods into the passenger cars of the Jinpu Railway express train. However, after the train arrived at the terminal station, customs inspectors, assisted by railway police and military police, removed the goods. Despite the Koreans' best efforts to protest, the goods were eventually transported to the customs warehouse for auction. (Reuters, 22nd)

(Tianjin) The Jinpu 305 train passed safely through Jinan this second night, some smugglers transported forty private goods to the station this evening, planning to load it on the train, they transported the goods back upon fearing the cut-off of customs official, in the past two months, this evening's southbound passenger train on Jinpu Railway was the calmest, travellers got to enjoy their seats with tickets purchased. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

All Motions Submitted to the Plenary Session Referred to Respective Special Committees for Deliberation

(4) The land price tax in Beijing will be implemented starting from the 25th year. The land improvement tax will be postponed. The estimation of the value of improvements should be completed within three years. During these years, the house tax in Beijing will be temporarily allowed to be retained, and should be levied at 70% of the original tax rate. Approved for record. (5) Passing the methods for controlling private radio stations set up by various agencies and public and private organizations, to be handled by the Executive Yuan. (6) Motions submitted by the Fifth Plenary Session of the Second Central Committee, to be distributed to various special committees for review. (7) Passing four budget proposals. ### Kong Xiangxi Discusses Promoting Income Tax Collection Method Intends to Adopt Reporting System Collection of Funds to Adopt Separate Responsibility System

(Nanjing) The Provisional Income Tax Regulations have been officially promulgated by the National Government. When the Central News Agency reporter visited Minister Kong yesterday, he inquired about how it will be implemented in the future. The main points of Minister Kong's speech are recorded as follows: Income tax is a good tax commonly used in various countries around the world. Our country has repeatedly discussed its implementation, but it has not yet been realized. Now that these regulations have completed the legislative procedures and have been officially promulgated by the National Government, they can be implemented immediately, which is a gratifying event. Considering that the income tax rates in various countries are high, for example, the most recent British system levies four shillings and sixpence per pound for the net income of each year starting from one hundred pounds, and an additional surtax is levied for those exceeding two thousand pounds. The US system levies 4% on the net income of each year starting from US$1,000, and from 5% to 59% when it exceeds US$4,000. The German system levies 10% on the net income of each year from 1,100 marks to 8,000 marks, and from 12.5% to 40% above 8,000 marks. The Japanese system levies tax on the net income of each year starting from 600 yuan, with tax rates ranging from a minimum of 8 per thousand to a maximum of 360 per thousand. At the beginning of its establishment in our country, the government, considering the people's hardships, set the tax rate at a lower level. As for the collection method, it is now planned to adopt a reporting system, with strict verification by government offices. If the report is not accurate, the state will impose strict sanctions according to law. Therefore, the procedure is quite simple, and methods such as prior registration and investigation will not be adopted immediately. This department is currently drafting the implementation rules, and soliciting the opinions of experts, scholars, and related organizations for research. Since income tax is most easily evaded, at the beginning of its implementation, the social environment should be carefully observed, and efforts should be made to meet the actual situation, so as to avoid cunning people from being spared by chance, and honest people from bearing the sole responsibility of paying taxes, which would defeat the government's original intention of promoting good taxes. The original purpose of the government is not the amount of tax revenue, but the vigorous reform of the tax system. Taxpayers should understand the government's intention of light taxation and honestly avoid deception, so as to express their sincerity in loving and saving the country. After the income tax is implemented, the income donations previously collected by the Central Party Department from public officials will no longer be levied. The government has already made a decision on this point. I have ordered the responsible personnel to strictly handle the collection of this tax in accordance with the following guidelines: (1) A new tax must be approached with new talents and a new spirit. All personnel must be selected through screening and examinations, and guaranteed. Emphasis must be placed on the training of young people, so as to utilize their energetic and enterprising spirit, and to prevent those with habits of laziness from mingling among them. (2) The collection and receipt of funds must adopt a separate responsibility system, so as to achieve the effect of mutual supervision. (3) Efforts should be made to save on the cost of collecting new taxes, and the procedures should be simplified. Finally, Minister Kong also said that at the beginning of the implementation of income tax, it is difficult for all measures to be perfect. It is hoped that all parties will provide more guidance. If there are brilliant opinions, I will accommodate them as much as possible, so that a good tax system can be promoted to perfection. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 22nd)

Total of Annulled Heavy and Miscellaneous Taxes in Various Provinces and Cities

(Nanjing) From the Fifth Plenary Session of the National Congress last year to the present, the Ministry of Finance has continued to receive reports from various provinces and cities on the abolishment of heavy and miscellaneous taxes. These include: Fujian abolished more than 2 million yuan in county regiment fees and surcharges, and promotion expenses; Gansu abolished more than 10,000 yuan in the third phase of heavy and miscellaneous taxes; Shandong abolished more than 150,000 yuan in the third phase of provincial and county local miscellaneous taxes, and reduced the surcharges on field taxes in eight counties, including Wudi, by more than 70,000 yuan. Together with the amount abolished before the Fifth Plenary Session of the National Congress last year, the total reaches more than 51 million yuan. The ministry will also pay special attention when reviewing the budgets of various provinces and counties in the future. All tax levies involving the nature of heavy and miscellaneous taxes will be corrected separately, so that local taxes and levies will gradually return to the right track, and the people's hardships will also be alleviated. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 22nd)

Regulations for the Organization of the Land Survey Bureau

(Nanjing) The revised full text of the Organization Regulations of the Land Survey Bureau of the General Staff Headquarters consists of thirteen articles. The main points are as follows: (1) The Land Survey Bureau is directly under the General Staff Headquarters and is in charge of the planning and implementation of national land survey and cartography. (2) The Bureau shall establish six sections: General Affairs, Management, Triangulation, Topography, Aerial Survey, and Cartography. (3) A Director shall be appointed to manage the affairs of the Bureau under the command of the Chief of General Staff, to oversee the Land Survey Bureaus in various provinces, the Central and Regional Land Survey Schools, and other relevant surveying matters. A Deputy Director shall also be appointed to assist in handling the affairs of the Bureau. (4) The Bureau may establish various survey teams, observation stations, construction sites, and repair shops as necessary for its business. (5) For the purpose of technical consultation and research, the Bureau may request the employment of consultants and the establishment of translation and compilation departments. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 22nd)

Central Observatory Discovers New Comet

(Nanjing) According to the Central Observatory, its director Yu Qingsong and researcher Chen Zunhui, after observing the solar eclipse in Japan, received a telegram from the International Astronomical Society stating that a bright star was discovered near the Cepheid variable star in the constellation Cepheus. The brightness at that time was magnitude 4, and it gradually rose to magnitude 1.5. On the night of the 21st, after the thunderstorm, around 2:00 AM, the weather cleared. Yu and Chen observed in the middle of the night and found that it had dropped to below magnitude 5. At the same time, a new comet was discovered in its vicinity, which is the first comet to be discovered this year, named Peltier. The brightness is magnitude 4, and the position is declination north 55 degrees, right ascension 23 degrees 5 minutes (in Cassiopeia, near several stars forming a W shape east of Polaris). It moves south by 2 degrees and the right ascension moves by 1 degree each day. On August 4th, the brightness may reach magnitude 3, making it the only comet visible to the naked eye in the past sixteen years. The central nucleus is very large, and the surroundings are cloudy with a tail, radiating light quite far. Once this comet disappears, it cannot be seen again for hundreds of years. The observatory is still continuing to observe and photograph its spectrum for spectroscopic research. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 22nd)

Our Country's Overseas Chinese Workers in Southeast Asia Smoking National Labour Bureau Suggests Improvement by Various Countries

(Nanjing) At this year's National Labour Conference, in view of the report "Opium and Labour" compiled by the International Labour Bureau, it was recognized that smoking by overseas Chinese workers in Southeast Asia is sufficient to hinder social and economic development and may increase mortality. It is believed that this scourge is caused by poor working conditions and state-run smoking establishments. It is suggested that various governments adopt improvement measures, the main points of which are as follows: (1) Reduce working hours, (2) Improve treatment, (3) Universalize sanitation facilities, (4) Workers' groups should have appropriate organizations. Its decision is that for those who are allowed to sell cigarettes in the colonies, the restriction methods are: (1) Opium is allowed to be sold to registered smokers, (2) Smokers must be registered, (3) Registration is limited to one year, (4) All registered smokers are not allowed to purchase cigarettes after five years, (5) The amount of cigarettes sold to licensed smokers should be reduced by one-fifth each year, (6) Establish smoking cessation hospitals, (7) Formulate a five-year smoking ban plan, (8) Prevent workers from buying and smoking private cigarettes. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 22nd)

China and Siam Negotiate Economic Cooperation

(Nanjing) According to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, Ling Bing, the head of our country's delegation to Siam, proposed concrete opinions on Sino-Siamese economic cooperation when he met with the Siamese Minister of Economy last month. (1) It is hoped that Siam and China will mutually seek to develop trade. (2) Develop Sino-Siamese shipping through Sino-Siamese cooperation, focusing on central China. (3) Open large-scale banks with Chinese funds or Sino-Siamese joint ventures to help the development of Sino-Siamese trade. The Siamese Minister of Economy expressed great approval for these opinions, saying that besides the first item requiring the responsibility of the two foreign ministries, the second and third items are within the possible scope, and the ministry will do its utmost to assist and promote their realization. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 22nd)

Tianjin Rickshaw Merchants Petition the Municipal Government

(Tianjin) Regarding the issue of rickshaw operators resisting the British concession's rickshaw inspection fee, on the morning of the 22nd, more than two hundred rubber-wheeled rickshaw merchants carried a petition to the Social Bureau, requesting that they forward it to the British Public Works Bureau to negotiate the cancellation of the new inspection fee law. Section Chief Han met with them on behalf of the bureau and worked hard to address their concerns. The crowd then went to the municipal government to petition. However, the mayor's secretary was not present, so they dispersed without results. They plan to continue appealing on the 23rd. The British Public Works Bureau believes that the lack of rickshaws within the concession causes great inconvenience to transportation. They have ordered plainclothes detectives to lure and arrest more than ten rickshaw pullers. The vehicles were detained, and the people were released, and told to quickly pay the fees. (Special dispatch from the 22nd)

(Tianjin) According to Tianjin Social Bureau Director Ma Yanzhong, both sides have their own reasons regarding the rickshaw owners' resistance to the British Public Works Bureau's fees. The municipal government has ordered Section Chief Pan Yushu to visit the British authorities in a private capacity to mediate. The lack of a swift resolution to this matter has had a great impact on the city, with ten thousand rickshaw pullers unemployed, which is also a serious matter. On the 22nd, in order to maintain traffic within the concession, the British Public Works Bureau continued to order the public bus to increase its services, and also rented dozens of rickshaws at high prices, ordering street cleaners to temporarily pull them and solicit business on the streets. The bureau has been willing to resolve the matter peacefully due to the large losses incurred from the delay in resolution. (Special dispatch from the 22nd)

Zeng Yangfu Arrives in Jiangxi Yesterday

The section from Nanchang to Zhangshuzhen (the Nanping Road route under construction) is already being built, and the section from Zhangshu to Ganzhou is also being planned, only the section from Ganzhou to Shaozhou is yet to be planned. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 22nd)

Page 10

Japanese Army Department in North China to Directly Develop North China's Economy

Cangshi Road Construction Still in Limbo; Japanese Army Department Decides to Proceed Step by Step

Tianjin dispatch: The construction of the Cangshi Railway, despite much publicity, remains undecided. The Hebei-Chahar Political Council appointed Pan Yukui, the head of the Political Affairs Department, as the director of the Engineering Bureau. Pan expressed a passive attitude, remaining indecisive. The Japanese side intends that the total cost of the railway should be 20 million yuan. Apart from the Japanese side having priority investment rights, it will not allow any European or American countries to intervene. However, according to the plan, the Japanese side will provide materials instead of cash, with steel rails, vehicles, sleepers, etc., all supplied by Mantetsu (South Manchuria Railway), priced fairly. The Chinese side, in addition to land and labor, must raise cash, which can be sourced from government allocations or commercial collections. However, there is strong opposition to using funds from the Beining Railway, as the Beining Railway's annual income is limited. If it is forced to bear this huge sum, it will be difficult to raise funds, and there are concerns that construction may be delayed midway, affecting the project. Furthermore, the Beining Railway was originally built with British loans. Diverting its funds to the Cangshi Railway's construction costs would be tantamount to allowing British capital to join, which does not align with the principles held by the Japanese side. Therefore, this point has been repeatedly expressed to Chen Juesheng, the chairman of the Transportation Committee of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council. The Hebei-Chahar Political Council is currently facing financial difficulties. Apart from the Beining Railway's income, which can be used with the approval of the Finance and Railway Ministries, there are no other sources to provide funds. Consequently, surveying and planning are stalled. The project cannot commence immediately due to this unresolved issue. The Hebei-Chahar Transportation Committee and the Cangshi Railway Engineering Bureau have not actively prepared. The land for the railway's foundation was purchased from the people during the Beiyang government era. In 1930, the Ministry of Railways took over, dispatching four commissioners to be stationed within the Tianjin office of the Jinpu Railway Bureau, responsible for managing files and renting out land. They are still continuing this management. The Hebei-Chahar Transportation Committee and the Cangshi Railway Engineering Bureau have not contacted them for inventory. Recently, unscrupulous gentry from various parts of southern Hebei, colluding with ronin (masterless samurai), are soliciting shares everywhere under the name of the Cangshi Railway. The Transportation Committee has received numerous complaints from those who have been deceived and has ordered investigations from all parties. The Japanese Garrison Army Headquarters in North China, regarding economic development, realized that the distance was quite significant after Wang Kemin came north and met with Tashiro twice to exchange views. The Japanese side expected North China's economic industrialists to invest, with the Japanese side providing technical and material assistance. In reality, due to the general wealth and banking groups' distrust of the current situation, they perceive investment as still too risky. After Wang's return south, his return north is uncertain. The Japanese Ambassador to China's proposed economic cooperation with our government is also difficult to achieve concrete results for a time. The Army Department, considering the slow progress hindering future achievements, convened a meeting of resident military officers in Tianjin on the 20th of this month, presided by Commander Tashiro. In addition to listening to a report by senior staff officer Ishii Yoshie on attending the Shanghai military officer meeting, they discussed the point of economic development and decided to utilize the Economic Advisory Department attached to the Army Department to make it active, working in step with the Mantetsu Tianjin office to directly develop North China's economy. Even if the achievements are only a fraction, they will not be considered too small. This will be implemented after approval from the highest Japanese military headquarters. (22nd)

Rampant Smuggling in Wuhu

Over 10,000 Bags of White Sugar Being Dumped in Various Counties via Wuhu; Two Civilian Ships Caught Smuggling Hardware in a Single Day

Wuhu dispatch: Due to Wuhu's transportation connections, since smuggling became rampant in North China, there has been deep concern about its encroachment here. Various industry-based anti-smuggling teams have been strictly preventing it, but there is still a sense that prevention is difficult and sometimes impossible. The Xinyi Company, which emerged in response, has successively transported over ten thousand bags of white sugar to Wuhu. In addition to selling to local sugar merchants, it is also being dumped in inland counties such as Xuancheng, Nanling, Fanchang, Gaochun, Dangtu, Hexian, and Wuwei. As a result, sales of domestic sugar and Taikoo & Dutch sugar have significantly decreased. The sugar industry is suffering an indescribable blow, and everyone is lamenting. Recently, the general merchandise industry discovered a general merchandise store on the riverside, claiming to be capitalized by Japanese merchants, specializing in the trading of cube sugar and seafood, and not paying business tax. Therefore, it has been decided to sever all ties with it. Just as various industries were indignant, anti-smuggling teams successively uncovered two cases of hardware smuggling. Both were purchased wholesale from Shanghai and transported by hired civilian ships. One was the Yuandahe Hardware Store on Chang Street, owned by Chen Shaoyu, carrying thirty packages of electrical materials, thirty packages of fish oil, and one box of hardware and electrical materials. The other was the Dayoufeng Hardware Store on Guohuo Road, owned by Zhao Wenxian, with the entire ship fully loaded with hardware and electrical materials. The customs dispatched Jiang Xunsi Zhu Huanchao, along with customs officers and anti-smuggling inspectors, to inspect each item by speedboat. The cargo ships were taken to the customs for interrogation. Zhu Wenli, the escort of Yuandahe, was transferred to the Commissioner's Office by the Public Security Bureau for investigation. All sectors are paying close attention to this. Qian Zhongyuan, the chairman of the Hardware Trade Guild, has reported to the County Chamber of Commerce for assistance and is actively lobbying and explaining. (21st)

Songjiang

Robbery of Villagers in Longxing Township

Xu Shusong, a villager from the sixth village, Zhongjiajing, seventh bao, ninth jia, third household in Longxing Township, the first district of the county, is relatively well-off. He used to work as a rent collector for the Geng family in the city. Recently, due to the hot weather, he hired workers to thresh at night in order to sell the threshed rice at a good price. Yesterday (21st) at around 10 PM, as the workers were finishing their work and dispersing, suddenly seven or eight robbers, speaking with local accents, broke into the house. Each held iron rulers, flashlights, and other items as weapons. With three people acting as lookouts outside, they bound the homeowner Xu Shusong and searched for an hour, carrying away their loot and leaving. Afterwards, the homeowner reported the loss to the local police station and requested an investigation.

Wuxi

Shops Not Allowed to Close

Long Tiyao, the magistrate of this county, believes that during the validity period of the licenses held by local opium dens and smoking parlors, they should continue to supply licensed smokers with opium and smoking equipment without interruption. Since the strict implementation of smoker control, smokers must have designated shops to purchase and smoke from, and must not purchase and smoke at will. Therefore, unless shops are closed down or have special circumstances and report to the county for approval, they must not close on their own. It has been found that the Xinxing and Tiansheng smoking parlors closed briefly without prior notice and have been fined accordingly. This matter is crucial to the future of the prohibition laws. Yesterday, the county government issued a notice to all opium dens and smoking parlors.

Organizing an Anti-Smuggling Committee

The Wuxi General Merchandise Trade Guild, recognizing the increasing severity of rampant smuggling, convened its 19th Executive Committee meeting yesterday. The chairman, Zhu Fuming, resolved to: (1) Organize the Wuxi County General Merchandise Trade Guild Assistance Anti-Smuggling Committee, with all executive committee members serving as ex officio members, and Zhu Fuming elected as chairman. (2) Establish four sections: Investigation, Review, Public Relations, and Documentation, with Zhang Yunting appointed as director of the Investigation Section, Zhou Lvfu as director of the Review Section, Jiang Xikang as director of the Public Relations Section, and Xu Jianyun as director of the Documentation Section. Work will commence immediately to assist in cracking down on smuggling and to prevent it. A letter will be sent to the Chamber of Commerce for record.

Embezzlement Case in the Land Tax Office

Deng Jiqian, a clerk in the Fee Department of the County Government's Land Tax Office, recently reported his adopted son, Deng Gaozhang, for stealing string tickets and colluding in embezzlement. County Magistrate Long instructed Director Fang to conduct a secret investigation, and Deng Gaozhang, along with related individuals Zhou Xilun, Zhang Huisheng, Zhou Yinru, Zhu Shuqing, and Zhou Yuedu, were all summoned for questioning and detained. Deng Gaozhang is considered the most culpable, and Deng has confessed to embezzling over one thousand yuan. However, the old tickets from 1938 to 1935 have not yet been fully audited, so the exact amount of Deng's embezzlement is unknown. Once the audit is completed, the truth will be revealed, and they will be ordered to compensate the full amount. The detainees jointly submitted a petition to the county government, requesting bail. County Magistrate Long approved it and ordered each to provide a written surety of five thousand yuan. Currently, Zhang Huisheng, Zhu Shuqing, Zhou Yinru, and Zhou Xilun have found suitable guarantors and been released on bail, with the guarantors pledging that they will be available whenever summoned. If the guaranteed individuals evade being summoned, the guarantors are willing to bear the responsibility of compensating the full amount. Deng Gaozhang and Zhou Yuedu remain in custody due to their inability to find guarantors. It is heard that Zhou Yinru and Zhu Shuqing believe they have been falsely implicated by Deng and have hired lawyers to file lawsuits in court for legal recourse.

The County Government has scheduled the collection of the first installment of the 25th year's land value tax to begin on August 15th. Flood Victims Along the River Petition

Along the riverbanks of Yaodong Wolf Mountain in Tong County, the stone groynes on the river surface have sunk, and the violent impact of the high tide has caused severe collapses. Continuous days of storms and rain have exacerbated the situation, turning the riverbanks into "running horses." The flood victims from various embankments, supporting the elderly and carrying the young, have come to the city to petition the Party and government agencies for the swift implementation of rescue and protection projects.

Haizhou

Rampant Banditry in Ganyu

Ganyu County is adjacent to Shandong Province and is a haven for bandits. Several years ago, it completely transformed into a bandit world. Since the implementation of the Baojia system and repeated suppression by the Provincial Security Team, the number of bandits killed and who surrendered is not small. However, cunning bandits and those with serious cases have all fled to Shandong. Now that the green crops are growing, and because the Provincial Security Team has been transferred, escaped bandits have taken the opportunity to return to their hometowns to rob and kidnap. This happens from time to time (Recently, more than ten bandits from Batiaozhuang, Guowei Township, the sixth district, kidnapped five villagers, and a villager, Wen Yuan, from the sixth bao of Jinshan Township, was also kidnapped by bandits, who also shot and injured a water buffalo. At the same time, in Huandunbu, the fourth district, more than ten bandits suddenly appeared, firing shots near the district office and carrying off villagers. As a result, several villagers were kidnapped. On the border between the county and Tancheng County in Shandong, bandits have gathered more than two hundred people, causing panic among the population and a sense of impending doom).
