The Changjiang Piece Goods Gang - Stopped Loading for Export

Started loading Chinese merchant ships yesterday - First batch of goods shipped out by Hongyuan

The amount of piece goods and cotton yarn shipped from Shanghai to various ports along the Yangtze River every year is huge. The main destinations are Jiujiang, Hankou, Yichang, Shashi, Chongqing, and various places in Hunan. These piece goods and cotton yarn are mostly loaded onto ships of the Six Companies. Since July 1st, the Six Companies decided to implement a measure to measure the size of the piece goods and charge according to the newly set freight rates, which aroused the opposition of the piece goods customers and customs brokers in Shanghai, who refused to load the goods. It was not until the 9th that Chen Panjun, chairman of the Customs Brokers Association, repeatedly consulted with Shen Zhongyi, Wu Delin, Li Zhiyi of Sanbei, and Zeng Guangqing of China Merchants, that the extension of half a month was granted, and it was promised to appropriately reduce the freight rates and relax the size standards, and the accumulated goods that were obstructed were loaded first. On the 14th, Chen Panjun, in the name of representatives of customs brokers and customers, sent a letter to Taikoo Company, requesting that from July 15th, the size of the piece goods shipped to the Yangtze River should be based on 30 cubic feet per piece, as was the case for shipments to Chongqing. If the box exceeds 30 feet, the freight can be charged according to the set freight rate. Those shipped before July 15th will still be calculated at the original rate of 5 yuan and 7 jiao and a half for each 30 feet. After July 15th, each piece will still be 30 feet, and the freight rate may be increased to 7 yuan and a half. Taikoo Company did not clearly respond to this letter, and still insisted on calculating according to the size of 18 feet per piece (13 yuan and 6 jiao for 40 feet) set by the Six Companies, so a 30-foot box would have to be charged 10 yuan and 2 jiao for freight. As a result, both parties could not agree. In the past ten days or so, various parties have been mediating, but to no avail. Foreign shipping companies believe that the Six Companies have already made a decision and must implement the proposal. However, if there is room for accommodation, they ask the customs brokers and customers to load the goods as usual for the time being, and the size should be measured according to the new regulations, and the calculation of the freight should be left to the final decision. The customers were not satisfied with this proposal, because once the size and price were stated on the bill of lading, it would be difficult to recover in the future. Not only would the loss be huge, but it would be tantamount to implicitly recognizing the new regulations. The customers and customs brokers changed their plans and resolutely refused to load foreign ships. They sent representatives and pushed Chen Panjun and Ning Shao of Sanbei and China Merchants to negotiate with the three companies. From today onwards, the Yangtze River piece goods gang in Shanghai voluntarily refused to load all the goods onto foreign ships and completely switched to Chinese ships. However, they requested that the freight rate for the piece goods shipped before the Six Companies had fairly relaxed the size and reduced the fees would not be determined for the time being, and would be calculated when the solution was resolved in the future. The freight can be paid in advance, but the amount is not disclosed. At the same time, they also requested Sanbei and China Merchants to each release Shanghai-Hunan special liners every week, specifically for carrying Hunan piece goods. Sanbei has already complied and telegraphed Hongyuan, Hongheng, Hongli, and Hongzhen. Four ships will come to Shanghai and sail directly to Weisha, with one ship going to Hunan every Tuesday and Friday. China Merchants Bureau also dispatched Jiangda and Jiangjing. Two ships will sail to Changsha specifically. After the two issues were resolved, the customers automatically refused to transport the Yangtze River piece goods on foreign ships, starting yesterday. The first batch of piece goods, which were specially loaded on Chinese ships to the Yangtze River, was transported by the Sanbei Hongyuan轮船 (轮船) ship, which was exported yesterday, with a total of 400 to 500 pieces, worth about 130,000 to 40,000 yuan. This was to Hunan. Tomorrow, the China Merchants Bureau Jiangshun ship will also have a large batch of piece goods transported to Jiujiang, Hankou, and other ports. There are more than ten customs brokers in Shanghai who operate piece goods, including Xinchanglong, Xinchangyuan, Fuhe, Huiji, Luyanggong, Ruiji, and Yongan. When a reporter from this newspaper asked Chen Panjun, chairman of the Customs Brokers Association, how many pieces of piece goods (including Changsha) are shipped to the Yangtze River from Shanghai every year, Chen Jun said that although there are contractions from time to time due to market conditions, on average, there are at least 82,000 to 90,000 pieces per year. Calculated at an average price of 350 yuan per piece, the total amount should be more than 30 million yuan. If the average freight rate is 7 yuan per piece, then the annual amount is more than 600,000 yuan, which is an alarming number.

Senji and Other Companies Empty Jiawang Company

Municipal Social Bureau Dispatches Personnel to Investigate Thoroughly

Jia Zai & Mining Co., Ltd., located at No. 31, Fuyi Lane, Shengping Street, Foch Road, British Concession, recently convened an extraordinary meeting of shareholders in the name of the board of directors, and published advertisements in various newspapers. Shareholders Senji and others stated that the company had been organized for a long time, but had never convened a regular meeting of shareholders over the years, nor had it notified the shareholders of the business conditions. They were very isolated from the actual situation of the company. Therefore, they went to the company's general office to inquire about everything, but did not get any results. They also failed to prepare the company's articles of association, minutes of shareholders' meetings, annual settlement statements, etc., in accordance with the law. The shareholders believed that whether the company had been registered and how the board of directors was formed concerned the rights and interests of the shareholders, so they immediately requested the Municipal Social Bureau to thoroughly investigate. After receiving the request, the Bureau dispatched personnel to investigate and ordered the shareholders to be informed.

This City's Anti-Smuggling Association Sets Up a Secret Reporting Office

Announcing to All Sectors to Report Violations

The Anti-Smuggling Association of All Sectors in this City held its second executive meeting at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday afternoon and decided to set up a secret reporting office and announce to all sectors to reward secret reports in order to warn unscrupulous merchants. Details are recorded as follows:

Executive Meeting

The Association held its second executive meeting at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 2 pm yesterday. More than 20 people attended, including Cao Zhigong, Liu Zhongying, Zhang Yichen, Qu Zhenhua, Zhou Xuexiang, Zhang Xiaotong, (Yu Dai), Yu Yaoqiu, and Wang Manyun. Cao Zhigong presided over the meeting, and Zhu Yutao recorded it. After the formalities, the chairman first reported that the original plan was for Yu Qiaqing, Wang Jian, and other five committee members to visit Cai Kong to ask for instructions on the anti-smuggling policy, but because Yu and Wang were both away from Shanghai on business, it was decided to postpone the visit. After the report was completed, the following cases were discussed: (1) Announce to all sectors and solicit secret reports. It was decided to hand over the draft announcement to the Secretariat. (2) Send a letter to various groups and the Citizen Federations of the two special districts, ordering their subordinates to cooperate in the arrest. It was decided to pass it. (3) Set up a secret reporting box. It was decided to temporarily set up a temporary office of the Association. (4) Appoint a person in charge of secret reporting affairs. It was decided to appoint Cao Zhigong, Zhang Yichen, and Qu Zhenhua to be responsible with the Information Section. (5) Determine the temporary office of the Association. It was decided to set it up in the Citizen Federation of the First Special District, Tianhou Palace Bridge. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Announcement to All Sectors

For the sake of announcement, since the occurrence of smuggling incidents in North China, it has become increasingly rampant, obstructing our country's customs from exercising inspection and seizure, resulting in the spread of smuggled goods and the near bankruptcy of national tax revenue. The various groups in this city, in order to assist the government in detecting smuggling and maintaining its lifeline, resolved to establish an anti-smuggling association of all sectors at a joint meeting on August 24th, and elected Wang Xiaoji, Du Yuesheng, Yu Qiaqing, Huang Renzhi (Zhou Xuexiang, etc.) and 35 others as committee members, and has already started working. It is believed that our country's industry and commerce were originally in the budding stage, and this smuggling has made it impossible to maintain. This city is a major port in the southeast and the commercial center of the country. The water and land transportation is also very convenient. If we allow traitors and vagrants to use it as a base for smuggling, the consequences will be unimaginable. After the second executive meeting, it was decided to set up a secret reporting office (the address is temporarily located at the Anti-Smuggling Association of All Sectors in Shanghai, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Tianhou Palace Bridge) in order to arouse the public to assist the government in detecting smuggling and unscrupulous merchants. The Association will advocate in good conscience, do its best to investigate and report to the government, and strictly keep the names of secret reporters confidential. As for the government's measures to reward the public for detecting smuggling, it will also be responsible for handling them. We hope that all citizens will rise up together to save the country from danger. This is a special announcement.

London, July 21st (Reuters) – Australia defeated Germany 4-1, winning the Davis Cup and securing the right to host the tournament. The hosting tournament will commence on July 25th.

McGrath replaced Quist and first defeated Hügel, 6-3, 5-7, 6-4, 6-4.

Kramm was originally expected to defeat Crawford, but due to a recurrence of a hurricane-related injury, he was replaced by Hügel. Crawford won 6-3, 6-1, 6-4.

Australia defeated England in 1907 to win the Davis Cup and held it for six years. The last time was in 1919.

If Quist can recover quickly, Australia has a great chance of winning the Davis Cup.

Education News: Unregistered High School Graduates: Preliminary Entrance Exam Date Determined: Supplementary Exams for Schools Entrusted from Other Provinces and Qualifying Exams for Mongolian and Tibetan Schools to Be Held Simultaneously: Dates Set for the 27th and 28th of This Month

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education will hold graduation examinations for schools entrusted by various provinces and cities, and to assist graduates from unregistered private high schools in the city, it has scheduled a preliminary entrance exam. The qualifying exams for some Mongolian and Tibetan schools will also be held simultaneously on the 27th and 28th of this month. To gather diverse opinions on the supplementary exams and the preliminary entrance exam, the Bureau Director has appointed Chen Bai, Xie Enfu, Zhang Yongchun, Tao Guangchuan, Gu Zhongyi, Liao Shicheng, Tang Yanxi, Hu Xiangchen, Shen Xiongqing, Qiu Zumu, and others as committee members to organize a committee to discuss all matters related to the proceedings. All exam regulations, information for candidates, information for proctors, and exam locations and schedules have been drafted separately and are listed below.

Time and Location

Mongolian and Tibetan School Graduates

Qualifying Exams: July 27th, 8:00 AM to 10:00 AM, Chinese Language; 10:20 AM to 12:20 PM, Party Principles; 1:30 PM to 3:30 PM, Mongolian/Tibetan Language; 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM, Northwest Geography. July 28th, 8:00 AM to 10:00 AM, Border Issues; 10:20 AM to 12:20 PM, Teaching Methods; 1:30 PM to 3:30 PM, Educational Psychology; 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM, Educational Statistics. Location: The school on Longhua Road.

Preliminary Entrance Exam: July 27th, 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM, Chinese Language; 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM, Mathematics; 3:30 PM to 5:30 PM, Physics and Chemistry, Geography and History, Psychology and Education. July 28th, 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM, Foreign Language; 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM, Vocational Subjects.

Supplementary Graduation Exams: July 27th, 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM, Chinese Language; 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM, Mathematics; 3:30 PM to 5:30 PM, Physics/Chemistry or General Introduction to Education. Those taking only Physics or Chemistry should be included. July 28th, 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM, Foreign Language; 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM, History/Geography. Those taking only History or Geography should be included; 3:30 PM to 5:30 PM, Party Principles or Biology or Principles of Physical Education. The location for both exams is Wuben Girls' High School on Huangjiaque Road, Ximen.

Exam Regulations

Candidates must enter the exam hall with their admission ticket before the scheduled exam time. Those arriving more than five minutes late will not be allowed to enter and will be marked as absent.

Candidates must bring a writing brush, inkstone, or fountain pen and ink, as well as arithmetic tools for the mathematics section. Other items are not allowed inside. (Except for drawing, where pencils are allowed, pencils are generally prohibited.)

Candidates must sit in the assigned seat according to their admission ticket number and are not allowed to change seats.

Each candidate will only be issued one exam paper and may not exchange it.

Candidates may not arbitrarily ask questions during the exam. If a question is necessary, they must first raise their hand.

Candidates may not engage in talking, peeking, leaving their seat, bringing in unauthorized materials, copying, or having someone else take the exam for them. Violators will be penalized with point deductions or having their exam paper invalidated, depending on the severity of the situation.

If candidates need to temporarily leave the exam hall due to special circumstances, they must report to the proctor and obtain permission from the examiner before leaving.

Candidates must adhere to the specified exam time and are not allowed to extend it.

After each subject is completed, candidates must place their exam papers on the desk for the proctor to collect. Candidates must then leave the exam hall immediately.

Candidates must strictly obey all orders from the examiner and proctors during the exam.

Information for Candidates

Candidates must absolutely adhere to the exam regulations and all orders from the examiner and proctors within the exam hall. Violators will be penalized depending on the severity of the situation.

A bell will ring ten minutes before the start of each exam. Candidates should immediately enter the exam hall in order and take their seats according to their admission ticket number, waiting for verification.

Candidates must place their admission ticket on the desk for the proctor to check at any time.

A siren will sound ten minutes before the end of each exam. Candidates who have not finished their papers should quickly prepare to finish.

Candidates should rest in the designated rest area after leaving the exam hall. They should not lose their admission ticket and must return it after all subjects have been completed.

Candidates must provide their own meals and tea.

Candidates may not bring any books, papers, or other items into the exam hall except for necessary stationery.

Candidates must write their name or any other identifying marks on the exam paper; otherwise, the exam paper will be invalidated. They must place the exam paper on the desk for the proctor to collect. There is no need to hand in the exam questions or scratch paper, which must be attached to the exam paper and returned. They must not be taken out of the exam hall.

Information for Examiners

Examiners must wear badges.

Examiners must arrive at the exam hall thirty minutes before the exam time each morning. The exam questions will be delivered by personnel dispatched by the Bureau.

Examiners must instruct the proctors to strictly enforce all exam regulations and maintain order throughout the exam hall and handle any unexpected events.

Examiners must lead the proctors into the exam hall ten minutes before the start of each subject to inspect the candidates' entry and seating arrangements and pay attention to order. After the candidates are seated, they must check the candidates' photos and admission tickets before starting the exam.

Examiners must open the sealed exam questions on the spot at the start of the exam and distribute them to the proctors according to the number of candidates.

Examiners must instruct the proctors not to read or explain the exam questions' content.

Examiners must instruct the proctors to count the exam papers, seal them on the spot, sign and stamp them, and submit them to the Bureau's office after all subjects have been completed for the day.

Examiners must fill out all required forms in detail and submit them to the Bureau's office for verification.

The examination time must be strictly followed as stipulated; examiners may not arbitrarily advance or extend it.

If an exam hall is divided into two or more classrooms, the examiner must temporarily assign proctors to be responsible for each room. The examiner must inspect each room and oversee everything.

If any major incident occurs in an exam hall, the examiner must immediately inform the Bureau's office by telegram, which will then be forwarded to the committee chairman for handling.

Information for Proctors

Proctors must wear badges.

Proctors must arrive at their assigned exam hall thirty minutes before the exam each morning.

Proctors must strictly enforce all exam regulations and must not show any favoritism or leniency.

Proctors must enter the exam hall ten minutes before the start of the exam to inspect the candidates' entry and seating arrangements. After the candidates are seated, they must check the candidates' photos and admission tickets.

Proctors are responsible for distributing and collecting the exam questions and exam papers.

Before distributing the exam papers, proctors must explain to the students that the seal on the bottom of the exam paper must not be opened; violators will have their exam paper invalidated.

Proctors should not read or explain the content of the exam questions.

After the exam begins for each subject, proctors should check whether the candidates' photos and the numbers on their admission tickets match the seat numbers while patrolling the exam hall.

If a candidate needs to temporarily leave the exam hall due to special circumstances, the proctor should immediately obtain permission from the examiner and monitor the student's departure.

Proctors may not leave their post before the end of the exam for each subject.

Jiangsu Province High School Graduation Exam Results to Be Released Next Month: Overall Jiangsu Exam Results Are Good: Only a Small Number Will Not Graduate

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education is calculating the results of the provincial high school graduation exams. Most of the passing and failing results have been calculated. However, in light of the students' university entrance exam schedule, the department has allowed schools to send the diplomas of graduating students to the department for stamping. If the scores are passing, they will be stamped and returned first to prove eligibility for the entrance exams. The overall average scores have not yet been fully calculated and will be announced by the end of August. It is reported that the exam results are good overall, and only a very small number of students will not graduate.

Jiangsu Provincial Medical and Political College: Cultivating Health Administration Talent: Completing County Hospitals

In recent years, there have been many reforms in medical administration in Jiangsu Province, such as the establishment of the Huaiyin Jianbi Health Experimental Zones, the preparation for the Nantong Wuxi Health Offices, and the examination of the directors of the county opium suppression centers. The organization of the Provincial Health Education Committee and the Provincial Capital Health Education Committee are also significant events. Because the authorities pay equal attention to health administration and health education, all graduates from the first health administration and health education departments of the Provincial Medical and Political College have been assigned jobs, with demand exceeding supply. It has recently been reported that the Huaiyin Kala-azar prevention team and its branches, which will be established soon, will be staffed by graduates from the first rural medical and pharmaceutical primary service training class graduating from the college this summer. It has also been learned that the authorities intend to complete all county hospitals in the next fiscal year to promote medical facilities. The admission requirements for the second health administration department of the Provincial Medical and Political College this semester are graduates of public or registered private medical schools with specialized training in health administration. The aim is to cultivate basic talent for promoting public health in the province. In the future, staff members for these county hospitals and directors of health offices will be selected from graduates of the health administration department. Among the fifteen graduates from the first health administration department, two are currently directors of health experimental zones, one is a director of a health office, and one is a director of a veterinary disease prevention experimental zone. The rest are either section chiefs or health technicians, all able to use their talents to engage in public health work.

Shanghai Municipal Museum Publishes First Series of Books

Since its establishment, the Shanghai Municipal Museum has been actively engaged in collecting artifacts. The museum believes that the museum industry is still in its infancy in China. To instill museum knowledge in the Chinese people, it has invited experts both inside and outside the museum to compile a series of museum books. The series is divided into four categories: museology, history, art, and archaeology. The first phase will publish ten titles, all published by the museum. It is reported that the first title in Category A, "An Introduction to Museology," has already been published. This book is compiled by Chen Duanzhi and provides detailed explanations of the theories and implementation methods of museums, with examples. The book includes forty illustrations of famous museums in China and abroad and includes a survey of eighty museums in China and a list of over thirty famous books on museums in China and abroad, which is particularly valuable. Anyone engaged in museums, public education centers, farmers' education centers, botanical and zoological gardens, various exhibition halls, exhibitions, as well as school teachers and educational administrators should read this book. The entire book is 180,000 words long and is priced at one yuan to popularize it, only covering the printing costs.

One Year of Sichuan University

(1) (Chengdu Correspondence) National Sichuan University was formed in 1931 from the merger of two universities. Because it is located in the remote southwest, it has not been valued in the past. Since Ren Hongjun took over as president of the university last September, he has spared no effort to reorganize and reform the university. In just two semesters, the university has made significant progress. The Ministry of Education sent personnel to inspect the university last semester and concluded that "since the beginning of this semester, the university has vigorously implemented a full-time professorship system, reorganized the curriculum, improved the administrative organization, and economized on office expenses to focus on expanding facilities. The university has also earnestly implemented training and management matters, and the school's discipline is improving weekly. These achievements are highly commendable." The university's work this semester has progressed even further. It is rumored that the university plans to recruit students in Shanghai, Beijing, and Chongqing this year, which shows its far-reaching plans. Based on my personal observations, I will list the main points below for the reference of those who care about education in the southwest.

The University's Organization

The university originally had only three colleges: Arts, Sciences, and Law. This year, the Provincial Agricultural College was merged into the university, combining them into four colleges: Arts, Sciences, Law, and Agriculture. There are more than ten departments, including the Chinese Literature Department, Foreign Literature Department, History Department, and Education Department in the College of Arts; the Mathematics and Physics Department, Chemistry Department, and Biology Department in the College of Sciences; the Law Department and Political Economy Department in the College of Law; and the Agricultural College, which has not been divided into departments this year. It is said that next year, the university plans to establish four departments: Agronomy Department, Horticulture Department, Forestry Department, and Plant Pathology and Entomology Department.

New Campus Construction Plan

The university's old buildings were all dilapidated and unusable. Since Ren Hongjun became president of the university, he has obtained a grant of 1,630,000 yuan from Chairman Jiang for the university's reconstruction and equipment upgrades. In addition to allocating 1,400,000 yuan in Sichuan Post-Disaster Public Bonds and 30,000 yuan from the Sichuan Education Department, the central and Sichuan provincial governments will each contribute 600,000 yuan, which will be allocated evenly over three years starting in the 25th fiscal year. All of this has been reported in various newspapers. It is now heard that the 1,400,000 yuan in Sichuan Post-Disaster Bonds has been paid out in cash by Director Liu of the Sichuan Provincial Department of Finance at 75% of face value, totaling 1,050,000 yuan. It has also been decided that it will be paid out in four installments starting in May, and the first installment has already been received. The first new building—the library—is scheduled to begin construction this summer. In addition, the university's construction plan is entrusted to domestic architectural experts from the renowned architectural firms Jintai Company and Gongli Business Company, such as Ge Songsheng and Xi Fuquan, to design. All drawings have been completed, and President Ren is currently in Nanjing in May to hire Weng Wenhao, Zhou Yichun, Li Ji, Jiang Tingfu, and other gentlemen with experience in education and architecture to form a review committee to conduct a detailed review. The result is that the three colleges of Arts, Sciences, and Law will be jointly built on the old site of the Imperial City, using the Jintai drawings, while the Agricultural College will remain outside the East Gate, using the Gongli drawings.

Increased Hiring of Prominent Professors

Since the university implemented the full-time professorship system, the number of classes missed this semester has been very small. In addition, the university has hired prominent professors, such as Qian Yunong, Yang Yunkui, Zhang Yizun, Zhu Jianren, Ding Shan, Luo Rongzi, and Yang Qi, to teach in Sichuan and guide students in their research. The academic atmosphere has changed for the better. The university is continuing to hire many more famous professors, such as Zhang Zhenru and Wang Xiaoliang, who will be arriving soon.

Establishment of Scholarships and Loans

Because Sichuan Province has been troubled by years of unrest, the countryside is in decline, and many students with economic difficulties have dropped out of school halfway through, which is very pitiful. In addition to the free tuition policy, the university has established a student loan program this semester, allocating funds from the school's managed funds to be loaned out to help poor students, so as to avoid them dropping out halfway. It is estimated that 63 students have continued their studies this semester thanks to the loans, and the amount loaned out is over 1,100 yuan. It is planned to continue this program in the future so that poor students will not have to worry about dropping out of school due to financial difficulties. In addition, Chen Hengzhe first established the Zhuang Yunkuan Scholarship at the university in memory of his parents and to encourage future generations. The scholarship is 200 yuan per year and is awarded in two installments. This semester, the students who received the scholarship included Wu Tian and five others, all of whom are talented students at the university.

Expansion of Farms and Forests

The Agricultural College was originally the Sichuan Provincial Agricultural College. The affiliated farms and the Guanxian Wuyan Mountain Forest Farm cover an area of over 1,000 mu. In the past, they were abandoned and not managed due to a lack of funds and were leased out, which was very regrettable. Now, since they have been merged into the university, all tenants have been evicted and the land has been reclaimed for active management. In addition, over 300 mu of land have been newly purchased not far from the university outside the East Gate of Chengdu to serve as the college's fruit tree horticulture farm and animal husbandry farm for students' practical training. The university is also actively cooperating with the Sichuan Provincial Department of Construction, such as jointly running the rice and wheat testing farm, the Neijiang sugarcane testing farm, and the Sichuan Provincial Technical Soil Training Class. Professors Yang Yunkui, Mao Zongliang, Yang Ligong, and others from the university serve as the heads and deputy heads of these programs, respectively. At the same time, the university is cooperating with the Agricultural College of National Central University and the Central Cotton Improvement Institute to improve the cotton industry. In the future, this will greatly benefit the improvement of agriculture in Sichuan Province. (To be continued)

Commercial News: Finance: Weak Demand: Gold Market Initially Stable, Ultimately Weak

The gold market opened this morning with a rise in pure gold, leading to greater stability. However, weak demand made it difficult to sustain the gains, and despite a slight rebound later, the market ultimately fell by one cent. In the early morning, overseas silver markets saw London rise while the US remained flat. Large traders said that buyers were satisfied after the market closed, with forward silver prices in Montreux rising by five to ten cents. Exchange rates contracted slightly, and London spot gold rose by two pennies. The Central Bank's listing showed that both the British and American rates were flat. The Customs Gold Unit rose by two cents. The standard gold bar price was listed at 1128.3 yuan, a higher opening price. After opening, selling activity began, and long positions were closed, leading to a decline. The HSBC exchange rate listing showed that both British and American rates were flat. Large clients took advantage of the low prices to buy bars, which led to some stabilization. The silver equalization tax was announced with a rise of 0.25. Later, buying interest increased slightly, leading to a gradual recovery. However, after the rise, many traders sold off. At noon, the trend was mediocre. After recording the market conditions for the first half of the day,

The opening price this morning was 1132.8 yuan, up 0.5 yuan from the previous close. Fuxing, Yongqing, Fayong, Dingkang, Futai, and Yongding sold off, falling to 1.5 yuan. The HSBC exchange rate listing showed that both British and American rates were flat. Qianchang, Xiang, Fuxing, and Yong maintained prices, remaining relatively stable, but fluctuating. The silver equalization tax rose by 0.25. Xianghe, Hengyu, Qianchang, Xiang, Qiafeng, and Yong successively bought bars, gradually rising to 2.5 yuan. Dachangxiang and others were slightly late to the market. The noon close was 1132.2 yuan.

The closing price, according to the Central Bank's standard gold bar price listing, rose to 1128.3 yuan, an increase of less than four yuan based on the closing price. This was a smaller increase than the previous close, which was over one yuan. The book prices for this month were 1125 yuan, for August 1129 yuan, and for September 1132 yuan. The morning water rate was 1125 yuan. Red gold was priced at 8 yuan above, at 1140.8 yuan. The spot market was stable. Tianjin goods were priced at 11.75 yuan above, and cooked red gold was priced at 10 yuan above, but there were no transactions. Trading within the market was normal. In total, Qiafengyong, Qianchangxiang, Shengyuanyong, Hengyu, Wanxing, and Fuxingyong were on the buying side. Dingkangfu, Yuqingfayong, Dadecheng, and Yuanyong were on the selling side.

The market conditions for the first half of the day were calm. The opening price this morning was 1132.8 yuan. The highest price was 1132.8 yuan. The lowest price was 1131.5 yuan. The noon close was 1132.2 yuan, with fluctuations of 1.3 yuan. The total number of transactions for the first half of the day was 2,156 bars.

1,911 bars remain for this month, with nine long positions and nine short positions.

Slight Selling, Exchange Market Somewhat Looser

The exchange market was somewhat looser yesterday as buyers remained on the sidelines, and there were more spread trades. In the early morning, overseas news reported that recent rates in London rose by 0.0625, with forward rates unchanged. Forward silver prices in Montreux rose by five to ten cents. London spot gold rose by two pennies. The British rate against the US contracted by 0.25, the British rate against France fell by nine pounds, the American rate against the British contracted by slightly more than 0.25, and the American rate against France contracted by 0.125. The Central Bank's listing showed that both British and American rates were flat. The Customs Gold Unit rose by one cent. The exchange market opened this morning with the recent selling price of British exchange at one shilling, two pence, and 0.375. British exchange was at 30.125 yuan. Compared to the previous close, both British and American rates were flat. After the opening, although foreign firms raised the shilling, banks still filled orders, with little impact. The HSBC exchange rate listing showed that both British and American rates were flat. Later, although banks engaged in counter-trading, the trend was slightly looser due to weak buying interest and more spread trades. The silver equalization tax was announced with a rise of 0.25. After this, the situation fluctuated, but the market was still unable to rally by noon. The closing selling price for recent British exchange was slightly stronger at one shilling, two pence, 0.375, and the American exchange was at 30.125 and 0.1875, with both slightly looser compared to the previous market British and American exchange rates. Chinese merchants remained inactive except for spread trades. However, Japanese banks were slightly more willing to fill orders. The transactions for the first half of the day are recorded below.

In the British exchange market, the recent selling price this morning was one shilling, two pence, 0.375. McGeer sold 3.3125 to a foreign firm for September. Citibank Taiwan sold to Huabi at the same price for the same month. McGeer bought October at 0.25 and 0.3125. Shanghai filled spot orders at slightly stronger 0.375. HSBC sold 3.125 to Citibank for March. The closing selling price for spot and July was the same at one shilling, two pence, slightly stronger at 0.375. August was at 0.3125 and 0.375. Shen Bao Local Supplement - Casual Remarks on Shantytowns by Fang Kewen

Thanks to the resistance of over two thousand people armed with chamber pots and brooms, and the appeals for help, the shantytown residents of Eastern Shanghai have won a small victory, a temporary reprieve from demolition. This victory is temporary. When the extension expires, under the guise of "tidying up the city," those poor shantytown residents will still face a tragic fate.

In order to avert this tragic fate, and recognizing that the fall of the lip leads to the exposure of the teeth, the shantytown residents of the Eastern Muddy West have organized a Shantytown Association. At the joint meeting, the chairman proposed the following suggestions: (1) Expedite the construction of affordable housing so that every shantytown resident has a place to live; (2) Increase workers' wages and establish affordable factories; (3) Relax the regulations for rickshaw driver registration; (4) Shantytown residents should automatically organize into an association for systematic management; (5) Limit the increase in shantytowns; (6) Automatically conduct household registration surveys; (7) Implement baojia self-governance, with every ten households forming a group. If the first suggestion can be realized, and the shantytown residents have the financial means to live in the new housing, then suggestions (4), (5), (6), and (7) can be abolished. As for suggestions (2) and (3), aside from the third suggestion which is possible, the second suggestion is excessively idealistic. At present, the shantytown residents are living on three days of work or are even unemployed. As long as they have work, how can they dare to think about "increasing workers' wages"? As for establishing affordable factories, the existing factories are successively falling into a state of semi-shutdown. Whether affordable factories can be established is obvious and need not be further discussed.

Regarding the first suggestion, "expedite the construction of affordable housing," naturally we hope it can be "expedited" for the sake of "city appearance" and the "hygiene" of shantytown residents. However, even if the Public Works Department builds affordable housing, whether the shantytown residents have the ability to live there is still a question. According to the letter of appeal the shantytown residents made to the Citizens' United Association, it states: "Because the market is depressed, the economy is tight, and industry is declining... Because young people are working half a month out of the month, averaging four cents per day, relying on six dollars per month. If it is just one person, they can barely survive, but if there are old and young in the family, they have to use this little income to buy bean dregs and broken rice to cook with yellow vegetable leaves... If we are demolished and have to live in apartments, I am afraid it will be difficult to do, because the cost of three days of work is not enough to cover the rent..." From this, it is not difficult to see whether the shantytown residents can afford "affordable housing." Although the resolution of the Shantytown Association also has the clause "requesting the Public Works Department to expedite the construction of affordable housing to prevent the shantytown residents from being displaced," if the rent is not free or set extremely low, the "displacement" of the shantytown residents will likely still be unavoidable.

The second issue is "limiting the increase in shantytowns." Naturally, if the market improves, limiting the increase in shantytowns will not be difficult. Not only limiting the increase, but even "ordering demolitions" would not be a problem. If people can live better lives, who would want to live in dirty, dark shacks? However, under the current social organization, the hope of the market improving is so slim, almost a fantasy. Under internal and external troubles, natural disasters and man-made calamities, rural people are being driven to the cities, and urban workers are being swept into the tide of unemployment. Under the various aggressions of imperialism, China as a quasi-colony has formed a situation of total collapse. Who can "limit" the "non-increase" of shantytowns?

The shantytown issue is one link in the social problem. If the entire social problem cannot be resolved, then there will be no way to resolve it. The Fair by Lin Hao

This small, gray room is filled with suffocating depression: a faint, powerless ray of light penetrates through the windows covered in dust particles. The rooster crows fiercely, and the sound of "ooh ooh ooh" constantly disturbs this small village, everything seems to be exuding an active vitality. The light in the room is dim, making Houfa's face full of wrinkles even uglier. His brows are almost touching each other with worry, carefully chewing over his troubled face. No one would doubt that she harbors a lot of melancholy! In her heart! She carried a bowl, chopsticks, vegetable porridge, and other things from the stove, walked to the edge of the table where Houfa was sitting, and began to complain about her husband, nagging:

"I said, isn't it better if you don't go? With all the chaos and war, you'll be dragged off right away: Think, what will happen to us, mother and son? Mao Mao's dad, I'm really afraid of you going!"

"Woman, what do you know!" Houfa took the porridge and vegetables with both hands, rolling his eyes. "The public officials all said: This new batch of recruits won't be conscripting: Yesterday when I came back, I ran into Chief Hu Si on the street, and I asked him, and he said it was just rushing you to the fair, nothing like that: Old Ma, who strikes the night watch, also rang the gong. (Note: Ringing the gong means telling the villagers not to panic.) And…" He paused, lowered his head, and busied himself with the chopsticks scraping the porridge. Houfa's wife just stared blankly at him in a daze.

Zhaimao, sitting opposite Houfa, opened his round eyes, dragging his snot, gesturing and stuttering, "Daddy, are you going to the fair? To pick plums to sell again! You have to give me some when you come back, right? Red, red blood plums." Then, turning his head to his mother, he said, "Mom! Why don't you let Dad go? Dad earns money, we have food to eat, and even more plums! Hee hee." His mother suddenly slapped him: "Little monkey, what do you know?"

Houfa ate the porridge hastily, put down the bowl and chopsticks, casually wiped his mouth. He picked up his water pipe and tobacco pouch from the table, packed a pouch of tobacco, filled the pipe, and went to the stove to light the fire and smoke: He conveniently picked up two bamboo baskets in the corner of the wall, and found the carrying pole behind the door and went out. Houfa's wife hurried to the door: "According to me..."

"According to you, don't go! Woman, will money sprout wings and fly into our arms?" He glared fiercely at his wife, spat, hung the baskets on the ends of the carrying pole, and with a heave, got it onto his shoulder, then bit the water pipe in his mouth. He puffed hard and vigorously, then took off, heading towards A Gui's house. Mao Mao followed a few steps happily and then went back.

"Hey! A Gui, let's go!" Houfa shouted on the path in front of A Gui's door. There was no sign of A Gui, but A Gui's wife stuck her neck out from the door: "He went a long time ago!"

Houfa suddenly realized with a dawning understanding that A Gui had been lying to him when he said he would go to the fair together yesterday. He had already left on his own: That turtle son of a bitch, he wanted to get to the market early. Suddenly, he thought of Changgen, Fuchun, A Chang, Jinshui, and the brothers in Tangwan, who had all probably gone to the market: With so many people, it would be terrible, the market prices would rise step by step, and it would be difficult to do business; Thinking this, he quickened his pace, really wishing he could grow wings and fly there.

Here, Houfa's wife waited until the sun had set, but she still hadn't seen Houfa come home. The little deer in her heart kept jumping uneasily. Carrying Mao Mao, she bolted the door and went to A Gui's house. It just so happened that A Gui's wife came out from inside and immediately opened her mouth, "Sister-in-law A Gui, has your A Fei come home yet? Alas! It's really, it's bound to be ominous. I told him long ago that he couldn't go, he just kept saying there was no danger, with an evil mouth and an evil face, going: Saying that old Ma who strikes the watch rang the gong: Chief Hu Si also said he could go, not hesitating at all, you see: It's really not early! Still hasn't seen a shadow. Oh God! What kind of sin is this?"

"The spirit just came back! It's the common people who deserve to suffer, what kind of civil war is this again!"

At this time, two or three, three or five, scattered people on the street gathered in piles, talking like news. Soon, they formed a large group of thirty or fifty women, and their voices were chaotic like the sound of brushing horses in every household in the morning, sounding annoyingly, with occasionally a few high and sharp voices, these were the cranes among the chickens, sounding even more moving. The wife of that Changgen was a notable crane: "As I see it, not to say something unlucky, I'm afraid he's already been dragged away!"

Just like a prisoner facing the death penalty, everyone put on an unknowing, bitter face, you looked at her, she looked at that, quietly, silently for a while. However, they had the same terror in their hearts, the same anxiety, the same resentment, and the same doubts. But, Jinshui's wife, the well-known gossiper, broke the silence: "Let's go to Tangwan to see if they've come back. What's the use of standing here? It looks like they're definitely going to be dragged away."

Like a swarm of bees, they rushed there again, stretching their necks, staring unblinkingly.

"Someone's coming!" Someone with sharp eyes said, happy almost to the point of jumping up.

Nearly a hundred eyes widened. Look: - that's right, there's someone, running as fast as he can. (Hoping it's him.) Houfa's wife prayed silently.

When that person got closer, A Chang's father suddenly ran over and embraced him, saying:

"What's wrong, why are you in such a hurry?"

"They… they… were all dragged… dragged… away!" A Chang said breathlessly, "I… I was lucky… I slipped… away…"

The old man's face showed infinite comfort: His own child was fortunately unharmed.

But, like a bomb, it shattered everyone's hearts.

"Oh my God!"

"I told him he couldn't go!" Houfa's wife wiped her tears and cried.

"Heartless people!"

"Wah..." Mao Mao opened his mouth and cried too.

It got dark. The village was still filled with cries and curses.

The Story of Two Cents by Zhang Lin

Unemployed, I drifted back to Zhouyougang with a broken heart. We didn't talk much. My wife still had a pair of heavy eyes. The house was even more dilapidated.

Perhaps due to worry, my temper became violent. One day, I again asked my wife to get some rice from her mother's house. She refused. For some reason, fire burned in my heart. I beat my wife. My wife was forced to go with a bruised face to her mother's house. When my wife brought back two cents for me, I felt a surge of shame. I wanted to hold her and cry. We were both sufferers, both weak. After coming to my house, she had been living secretly like an abandoned dog, secretly working. This reckless vent! But I was again protected by the pride and self-defense that a man should have. I grabbed the money and went to the street to buy rice.

The sea stretched out quietly, mockingly shining with slight waves. I walked on the familiar dirt, looking at the shore where I had spent my entire childhood. Scenes flashed uncomfortably across my mind, disappearing happy images.

"Lou Lou, is that you? When did you come to the government seat?" Turning around, the person asking the unfamiliar question was a dark and thin face. I couldn't remember who it was, only that pair of sunken eyes, the same line-shaped eyebrows, still seemed a bit familiar.

"It hasn't been long! Alas, you don't recognize me anymore, Liansheng is my name!" Liansheng, since we parted, we haven't met once. For the sake of their own lives, these childhood friends gradually became estranged, gradually disappearing from the bottom of their hearts. Tonight's sudden encounter, I didn't know what to do.

"You're Liansheng! Oh, many years since we met, I really didn't recognize you. How have you been lately?" Seeing his clothes, I knew what his life was like.

"Me, alas, you see... You were living a good life in Shanghai?"

He laughed, pointing to his beggar-like clothes. He deliberately tried to laugh as if he didn't care, but the laugh only made him look more pitiful.

"I'm just getting by." I only shook my head negatively. In such a situation, it was certainly not permissible for me to complain.

We couldn't find anything to say, each looking at the sky, looking at the sea, two pairs of eyes avoiding each other. Two old friends who had been separated for eight years carried their own pain and remained silent.

"Me, have we been friends for many years?" He suddenly said with a bitter smile.

His eyes seemed excited, shimmering, turning red like the evening glow in a noodle shop. I didn't know what was going to happen, just nodded subconsciously.

"It's nothing," he said with an unnatural smile. "Lou Lou, I know your family isn't doing well either, but the acquaintances here are all scattered. I've been wandering on this island all year round, and I don't have a home either, alas, we have to be honest. I haven't eaten for three days. Can you give me two or three cents?" His eyes were even redder. In the reflection of the evening glow, I could see his hands shaking. His eyes dared not look at me, only deliberately averted to the distance.

"What do I do with these two cents?" I felt my face burning, my hands shaking. What to do? Give it to him? What about myself, what about my wife? We also haven't eaten for a day! If I don't give it to him, I can't be so heartless to eight or nine years of friendship. I took the two cents to the mouth of my pocket, to my chest, but my hand suddenly shrank back, looking at his small body like a stray dog. He turned his face, our eyes met again, but also immediately parted.

"Liansheng, I, I only have two cents, take it!" My fingers were trembling, my heart was jumping madly, suppressing my rapid breathing, I heavily took the two cents from the mouth of my pocket.

His face was strained, his eyes were staring at me like nails, flickering with suspicion. He suddenly pulled back his outstretched hand to take the money, and said hoarsely, "I shouldn't make things difficult for you, I understand. Haha, I remember, I have a place, a friend's house where I can get a meal. Thank you, we'll see you tomorrow!" He twitched his face as if smiling, and without waiting for my reply, he dragged his staggering steps and disappeared into the rice paddies below the embankment. I took the two cents in a daze and walked towards the street. Radio Drama

Mother of Abyssinia

The Italian army approached a certain village in Abyssinia. The villagers fought back furiously, destroying roads with explosives and diverting rivers, while launching guerrilla warfare.

The mother's son, of course, also followed all the young people to fight, leaving the mother, daughter-in-law and children at home.

The mother was a kind woman. She enthusiastically donated the money she had worked so hard for to the country, implementing Emperor Selassie's words:

If you have two pieces of clothing, be willing to donate one; if you have three meals a day, be willing to eat only two.

The mother also generously helped A Jinu, who owed someone money. She also earnestly told the young man: Really, police officer, how can you lock up young people at this time? Mara, you're not good either. How can you ask A Jinu for debts? Listen, the sound of cannons is so loud, everyone go to fight! Who made our family so poor? Isn't it the foreign capitalists? Let's ask them for debts!

Really, we will always have a day to demand this debt of blood from the enemy! Not someday, but today. Let's demand this debt of blood today! The young people also realized.

However, because the Abyssinians were enlightened, it made Daly angry and exposed the bestial nature of the massacre even more nakedly. Airplanes, cannons, machine guns, poison gas, further oppressed the body of Abyssinia.

However, airplanes, cannons, machine guns, and poison gas cannot eliminate the Abyssinians' heart to save the country. Instead, it increased their courage to resist and strengthened their national salvation will. The enemy also dropped despicable and absurd leaflets. Neighbor B and others picked them up at the mother's house and discussed surrendering. Just as her son came back and heard the words of surrender, he angrily killed Neighbor B. The son roared loudly at the people: We only have one way, and that is to resist, to resist desperately!

At this time, the enemy launched a large-scale attack. The traitors also realized that surrendering would also lead to death, and seeking the League of Nations was useless, so they had to resist desperately.

The war became more intense. All the oppressed people of the world, such as the people of Italian Somaliland and the working people of Italy, also felt their own oppression and spontaneously rose up to help the people of Abyssinia.

The two races also fought more bravely - the son was killed in battle, and the daughter-in-law filled the gap. The traitors came, and everyone exposed their theories of national funding and jointly attacked the traitors. Eliminating the national traitors is just… Even if… came

Petition to Party and Government by All Workers of Hongxing Hosiery Factory Yesterday

According to the Dagong News Agency, the Hongxing Hosiery Factory on Cai Shi Road in the French Concession, under the pretext of processing worker registration, announced a shutdown at the end of last month. After mediation by party and government organs, it was limited to resume work on the 20th. When the time came, the factory insisted on dismissing eight union directors, which aroused the indignation of all workers and has not been resolved for many days. Now the factory employs workers and deceives superiors. Upon hearing the news, all workers were panicked and set off yesterday in different directions to petition. The details are recorded below.

Petition by All Workers: The factory originally scheduled to resume work on the 20th of this month, and at that time posted a notice dismissing eight enthusiastic union directors, including Deng Yixin and Shi Xiuying, refusing them entry to the factory, which aroused the indignation of all workers. They refused to enter the factory to work and quietly waited for the party and government organs to mediate according to the law. Because the factory saw that the workers refused to resume work, it instructed Li Youpei, a senior factory official, to hire more than 20 workers to petition the party and government organs yesterday morning, intending to obscure everything. Upon hearing the news, the workers were panicked. More than 300 people gathered in the Tangjiawan Assembly Hall and set off in batches to petition the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau, and presented the truth in person. Li Weixiong of the Municipal Party Department and Wang Xianqing of the Social Affairs Bureau received them and replied that they considered the factory's unreasonable dismissal of workers inappropriate and instructed the workers to wait quietly for mediation and not to cause other incidents. They had to leave at one o'clock in the afternoon, and in the afternoon, they went to petition Du Yuesheng, Lu Jingshi, and Zhou Xuexiang, the acting chairman of the General Labor Union.

Petition for Relief: The Second District Knitting Industry Union yesterday submitted a petition to the party and government organs for relief regarding the dispute at the Hongxing Hosiery Factory. The original petition stated, "In order to request the Hongxing factory to be ordered quickly not to dismiss Shi Xiuying and other eight people unreasonably, and to quickly withdraw the criminal prosecution, and not to create unnecessary complications, to quell public anger and resolve the incident. The union previously reported to your (union) (bureau) for verification and handling regarding the unreasonable dismissal of Shi Xiuying and other eight people by the Hongxing factory. Now, the union examines the public sentiment and finds it truly indignant. Numerous reports have been received stating that the Hongxing factory at this time is resorting to any means, secretly sending its confidant and running dog Li Youpei to secretly buy off workers with heavy prices, conspiring to create labor disputes to achieve its private ends. The union members and workers are extremely indignant upon hearing this. If they are not comforted soon, accidents may be unavoidable. Therefore, we urgently submit this petition, dispatching Zhang Zhuyun, together with more than 300 union members and workers of the Hongxing factory, directly petitioning your (union) (bureau), requesting that the Hongxing factory be quickly ordered not to dismiss workers unreasonably, and to quickly withdraw the criminal prosecution, and not to create unnecessary complications, to quell public anger and resolve the incident, which would be in the public interest."

Telegram to President Jiang: An urgent telegram to Chairman Jiang of the Military Affairs Commission. The Hongxing Hosiery Factory in Shanghai, this time, due to failing to fulfill the work resumption notice and printing illegal characters such as "shall be subject to the most severe punishment" to force workers to register, caused a dispute. The responsibility for this has long been determined by the municipal party and government. For more than ten days, the factory has not come to its senses and has colluded with former important officials in the Social Affairs Bureau to carry out extensive activities, and illegally dismissed eight workers, secretly sending its confidants to buy off labor traitors with heavy money, conspiring to make trouble, hoping to achieve its private goals of destroying the labor movement, disregarding the country, and using industry as a last-ditch gamble, which is extremely absurd and perverse. Your Excellency cherishes the people, and the people are grateful. All citizens should be careful and comprehensive, considering the overall situation, so that they can extricate themselves from difficulties and hardships. Now, the Hongxing factory is not hesitating to do this, which is extremely heartbreaking. I implore Your Excellency to show compassion and to show the majesty of national law with the wrath of thunder, ordering the municipal party and government to order the Hongxing factory not to dismiss workers, to stabilize society and benefit the people's livelihood. This would be most fortunate. Shanghai Second District Knitting Industry Union respectfully.

Inspection Report of the Central Bank

The 292nd inspection report of the Central Bank's convertible note issuance reserve states: In accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, this committee is responsible for inspecting the number of convertible notes issued by the bank and the remaining reserve. The 292nd inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on July 18, 1936, and the results of the inspection are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued is 30,046,7285 silver dollars, including 26,923,9873 silver dollar notes and 3,122,7412 auxiliary coin notes. The total amount of convertible note reserves is 30,046,7285 silver dollars, including 20,180,04385 silver dollars in cash reserves. This cash reserve includes 10,149,49751.86 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuing headquarters, branch libraries, and various branches, and 9,685,4633.14 silver dollars stored with counterparts. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 9,866,2900 silver dollars. (B) Regarding the total amount of convertible notes issued, 400,9630.07 customs gold units, and the total amount of convertible note reserves in customs gold units is 400,9620.07 customs gold units. This reserve includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68, totaling 400,9630.07 customs gold units. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve should be at least 60%, and the remainder should be a guarantee reserve of legal guaranteed products. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guarantee reserve is within 40%. This is in accordance with the regulations. This is specially reported. July 20, 1936, Li Fuxun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank; Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiqu.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The Shandong area and the Yellow Sea are cloudy with showers and strong northeasterly winds. The upper and middle reaches of the Yellow River and the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River are partly cloudy and quite hot with unpredictable light winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy with strong northeasterly to northwesterly winds and slight showers. The East China Sea, Kyushu, and southern Korea have cyclone rainstorms due to the northward movement of the hurricane. The Taiwan area is cloudy with strong southwesterly winds. The center of the hurricane at 2:00 PM was within 60 miles of 21 degrees north latitude and 127 degrees east longitude, moving northwest-west or north-northwest with strong winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 92.8 and the lowest was 74.8. On the same day last year, the highest was 91.9 and the lowest was 77.5.

Olympic Torch Relay Passes Corinth Canal Bridge, Residents Along the Way Enthusiastically Welcome and Celebrate

Olympia, 20th (National Electric) The Olympic torch relay, with 3,000 runners each running one and a half miles, continues in a very solemn performance. The first section of this 1,837-mile relay will be completed by Condylis of Greece. Afterwards, it will pass through six countries including Greece, Bulgaria, Yugoslavia, Austria, Czechoslovakia, and Germany. The final torch will be carried into the Berlin Olympic Games by Louis of Greece, the winner of the marathon race held in Athens in 1896. He will complete the final section of the relay at 4:00 PM on August 1st.

Athens, July 21st (National Haitong Du Electric) The Olympic torch relay continued all night yesterday, passing through the rugged roads between Mount Loponi and Sas, and then out onto the plains. The villages and towns along the way were warmly welcomed. The torch may reach Corinth by noon today. The first ceremony en route will be held at the altar built on both sides of the public market here. Tonight, the torch may reach Athens. Bishops and priests will wear ancient Greek robes to welcome the torch. The Greek celebration of the Olympic Games will be held in Athens.

Athens, July 21st (National Haitong Du Electric) The torch relay, which departed from Mount Olympus, arrived here this afternoon. The crowd of spectators was huge. King George II of Greece, cabinet members, and other domestic dignitaries were waiting on a specially constructed observation platform to witness the arrival of the torch and participate in the celebration ceremony. When the runner holding the torch arrived at the Parthenon, a priest stood up and lit a lamp on the altar in front of the Parthenon. The light of this lamp will not be interrupted until the closing of the Olympic Games. Then, he blessed the torch, saying, "The spirit of ancient Olympus is still immortal. May the light of this torch shine forever and illuminate the nations participating in the Olympic Games with the light of peace. Before this temple of Pallas Athena, on the sacred stone of the Acropolis, I wish heaven to bless the athletes of the 11th Olympic Games in this city."

After this blessing, the torch was carried by a runner to the Athens stadium, where a similar ceremony was held. By the time the second runner carried the torch to Delphi, it was already night.

At 11:30 this morning, the ancient Olympic torch arrived in Corinth, where the residents gathered in the public market to welcome it. There were also residents watching along the way. The church bells rang loudly when the torch arrived. The runner handed the torch to the mayor, who lit the lamp of the altar in front of the city hall with the torch. At the same time, the military band played the Greek national anthem. The public market was decorated with the national flags of Greece and Germany. There were also 30 young Greek women performing national dances in front of the altar.

At 12:50, the torch passed over the bridge of the Corinth Canal. This bridge connects the mainland with Loponiirus. This is also the location of King Pelops in mythology. The origin of the Olympic Games is also based on this. King Pelops, in the past Olympic Games, was actually part of the funeral. It is said that it was first held after the death of King Pelops.

World Games Football Opening Match: USA vs. Italy, August 3rd, 4:00 PM

Berlin, 21st (Allied Electric) The Olympic football preliminary round combination has been decided. On the third day of the Games, August 3rd, at 4:00 PM, the match between the USA and Italy will be the starting point. Afterwards, two matches will be held daily in the football field. After the semi-finals, they will be held in the Olympic Stadium. Japan will play its first match on the 4th against Sweden. Sweden is a strong team in Northern Europe and has played against Germany many times. So far, Sweden has won six and lost four. It is said that Germany has a slight individual advantage this year.

Olympic Marathon Route Determined: More Than 42,000 Kilometers

Berlin, 21st (Haitong Electric) The distance of the Olympic marathon race, scheduled to be held on August 9th, will be 42,195 kilometers. Starting from the Olympic Stadium, it will proceed along the shore of Lake Halvel, then onto the Affers automobile road, reaching the halfway point, and then returning along the same route.

Starting at 3:00 PM, it will take about two and a half hours. The reason for choosing this route is to minimize the amount of sunlight the runners are exposed to.

The entire route is marked with white powder, and each section is marked with numbers indicating the number of kilometers to the finish line. High towers have been built at intersections, and obstacles at corners have been removed. Although this route does not have the difficulties of the original route between Marathon and Athens, it is a major test of the endurance of the athletes.
